# <a name="using-the-performance-analysis-of-logs-pal-tool"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-102">使用記錄檔 (PAL) 工具的效能的分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-102">Using the Performance Analysis of Logs (PAL) Tool</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-103">PAL （效能分析的記錄檔） 工具讀入效能監視器計數器記錄檔 （任何已知的格式），並且會使用複雜，但已知臨界值 （提供） 加以分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-103">The PAL (Performance Analysis of Logs) tool reads in a performance monitor counter log (any known format) and analyzes it using complex, but known thresholds (provided).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-104">此工具會產生 HTML 基礎報表，以圖形方式圖表重要的效能計數器，並擲回警示時已超過閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-104">The tool generates an HTML based report that graphically charts important performance counters and throws alerts when thresholds are exceeded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-105">臨界值最初根據 Microsoft 產品團隊，包括所定義的臨界值[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]，而且屬於 Microsoft 支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-105">The thresholds are originally based on thresholds defined by the Microsoft product teams, including [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)], and members of Microsoft support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-106">此工具不是傳統的效能分析的取代，但它會自動分析的效能計數器記錄足以協助節省時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-106">This tool is not a replacement of traditional performance analysis, but it automates the analysis of performance counter logs enough to help save you time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-107">PAL 工具：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-107">The PAL tool:</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-108">分析臨界值的效能計數器記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-108">Analyzes performance counter logs for thresholds</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-109">很大的效能記錄檔</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-109">Is helpful for large Perfmon logs</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-110">識別[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]和作業系統效能計數器瓶頸，藉由分析臨界值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-110">Identifies [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] and operating system performance counter bottlenecks by analyzing for thresholds</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-111">擴充，以進行分析上的任何效能計數器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-111">Is extensible to do analysis on any performance counters</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-112">可用來協助撰寫您自己的計數器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-112">Can be used to help write your own counter</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-113">PAL 是在免費下載[ http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98098 ](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98098)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-113">PAL is available as a free download at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98098](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98098).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-114">它需要 Microsoft 的記錄檔剖析器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-114">It requires Microsoft Log Parser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-115">記錄檔剖析器是功能強大、 靈活的工具，提供通用的查詢文字為基礎的資料，例如記錄檔、 XML 檔案和 CSV 檔案，以及索引鍵的資料來源來存取 Windows 作業系統，例如事件記錄檔、 登錄、 檔案系統和作用中Directory® 目錄服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-115">Log Parser is a powerful, versatile tool that provides universal query access to text-based data such as log files, XML files, and CSV files, as well as key data sources on the Windows operating system such as the event log, the registry, the file system, and Active Directory® directory service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-116">若要使用此工具來查詢大量的記錄資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-116">You may want to use this tool to query a significant amount of logging information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-117">您可以下載記錄檔剖析器工具在[ http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=85574 ](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=85574)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-117">You can download the Log Parser tool at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=85574](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=85574).</span></span>  
  
## <a name="using-pal-with-performance-counter-logs-in-different-languages"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-118">在不同的語言使用 PAL 與效能計數器記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-118">Using PAL with Performance Counter Logs in Different Languages</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-119">PAL 工具會分析僅以英文語言的效能計數器記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-119">The PAL tool analyzes performance counter logs only in English language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-120">若要使用其他語言中的效能計數器記錄檔 [PAL] 工具，您必須先轉換記錄檔，以英文語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-120">To use the PAL tool with performance counter logs in other languages, you must first translate the logs to English language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-121">您可以使用**Perfmon 記錄轉譯程式**工具位於[ http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=158802 ](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=158802)翻譯成英文原始的效能計數器記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-121">You can use the **Perfmon Log Translator** tool available at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=158802](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=158802) to translate the original performance counter log files to English.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="understanding-the-pal-tool-report-for-microsoft-biztalk-server-2010"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-122">了解 Microsoft BizTalk Server 2010 的 PAL 工具報告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-122">Understanding the PAL Tool Report for Microsoft BizTalk Server 2010</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-123">PAL 工具提供 Windows 作業系統，Microsoft SQL Server，效能監視器記錄分析臨界值和[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-123">The PAL tool provides Perfmon log analysis of thresholds for the Windows operating system, Microsoft SQL Server, and [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-124">本章節描述大部分的 BizTalk Server 閾值報表 PAL 工具中分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-124">This section describes most of the analyses in the BizTalk Server threshold report in the PAL tool.</span></span>  
  
> [!NOTE]  
>  <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-125">本主題很長，以便可以在一個地方，以方便參考包含有關 PAL 工具的完整資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-125">This topic is long so that comprehensive information about the PAL tool can be contained in one place for easy reference.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-126">PAL 工具會報告下列分析和臨界值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-126">The following analysis and thresholds are reported by the PAL tool.</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-127">分析的類型和名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-127">Analysis Type and Name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-128">分析描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-128">Analysis Description</span></span>|  
|----------------------------|--------------------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-129">： 磁碟的磁碟可用空間的核心傾印</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-129">Disk: Disk Free Space for a Kernel Dump</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-130">這項分析會檢查以確定有足夠的磁碟空間，用於作業系統磁碟的所有記憶體傾都印。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-130">This analysis checks to make sure there is enough free disk space for the operating system to dump all memory to disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-131">如果可用磁碟空間不足，作業系統將無法建立 memory.dmp 時，這是要分析根本原因的核心傾印檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-131">If insufficient disk space is available, then the operating system will fail to create a memory.dmp, file which is necessary to analyze the root cause of a kernel dump.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-132">磁碟： 邏輯/實體磁碟介面分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-132">Disk: Logical/Physical Disk Interface Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-133">這項分析會查看每個實體磁碟的閒置時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-133">This analysis looks at the idle time of each of the physical disks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-134">多閒置磁碟，使用磁碟越低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-134">The more idle the disk is, the less the disk is being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-135">此計數器適合在使用一個磁碟的邏輯磁碟中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-135">This counter is best used when one disk is used in the logical disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-136">"%閒置時間 」 報告的範例間隔期間磁碟閒置時間百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-136">“% Idle Time” reports the percentage of time during the sample interval that the disk was idle.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-137">參考： 統治出磁碟繫結的問題 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-137">Reference:  Ruling Out Disk-Bound Problems at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-138">磁碟： 邏輯/實體磁碟讀取/寫入延遲分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-138">Disk: Logical/Physical Disk Read/Write Latency Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-139">Windows 偵測到磁碟的效能瓶頸最可靠的方式是藉由測量其回應時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-139">The most reliable way for Windows to detect a disk performance bottleneck is by measuring its response times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-140">如果回應時間大於.025 （25 毫秒為單位），也就是保守的臨界值，然後值得注意的速度並影響使用者的效能問題可能會發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-140">If the response times are greater than .025 (25 milliseconds), which is a conservative threshold, then noticeable slow-downs and performance issues affecting users may be occurring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-141">如需詳細資訊，請參閱邏輯/實體磁碟讀取/寫入延遲分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-141">For more information, refer to Logical/Physical Disk Read/Write Latency Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-142">磁碟： Logical Disk Transfers/sec</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-142">Disk: Logical Disk Transfers/sec</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-143">「 磁碟 Transfers/sec"是讀取的速率和寫入磁碟上的作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-143">“Disk Transfers/sec” is the rate of read and write operations on the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-144">這項分析檢查以查看是否有任何的邏輯磁碟的臨界值會顯示不佳的回應時間 （大於 25 毫秒 I/O 作業的回應時間）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-144">The thresholds for this analysis check to see whether any of the logical disks are showing poor response times (greater than 25 ms response times for I/O operations).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-145">如果為 true，則每秒磁碟轉移操作應該等於或高於 80。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-145">If this is true, then the disk transfers per second should be at or above 80.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-146">如果沒有，則需要調查磁碟架構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-146">If not, then the disk architecture needs to be investigated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-147">不佳的磁碟 I/O 的最常見原因是多載 SAN 上的 LUN。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-147">The most common cause of poor disk I/O is LUN overloading on the SAN.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-148">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 Logical Disk Transfers/sec 本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-148">For more information, refer to Logical Disk Transfers/sec in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-149">磁碟： LogicalDisk %可用空間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-149">Disk: LogicalDisk % Free Space</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-150">「 %可用空間 」 是已在所選邏輯磁碟機上可用的總可用空間百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-150">“% Free Space” is the percentage of total usable space that was free on the selected logical disk drive.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-151">少於 30%的可用磁碟空間之前，應該不會影響效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-151">Performance should not be affected until the available disk drive space is less than 30 percent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-152">使用磁碟機的 70%時，剩餘的可用空間是磁碟的位於更接近中間，都是磁碟的在較低的效能層級運作的磁碟磁針。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-152">When 70 percent of the disk drive is used, the remaining free space is located closer to the disk's spindle at the center of the disk drive, which operates at a lower performance level.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-153">可用磁碟空間不足可能會造成嚴重的磁碟效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-153">Lack of free disk space can cause severe disk performance.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-154">參考： NT 伺服器和磁碟子系統效能 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-154">Reference:  NT Server and Disk Subsystem Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-155">磁碟： 處理 IO Data Operations/sec 和處理 IO 其他作業數/秒分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-155">Disk: Process IO Data Operations/sec and Process IO Other Operations/sec Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-156">這些計數器計算所有的 I/O 活動，包括檔案、 網路及裝置 I/o 處理序所產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-156">These counters count all I/O activity generated by the process to include file, network and device I/Os.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-157">當處理序正在執行超過 1,000 個我 / O 的每秒，並且將它標示為警告，請檢查這些分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-157">These analyses check when processes are doing more than 1,000 I/O’s per second and flag it as a warning.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-158">這些分析最適合用於與其他分析，例如磁碟分析相互關聯來判斷哪些處理程序可能會陷入 I/O 活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-158">These analyses are best used in correlation with other analyses such as disk analysis to determine which processes might be involved in the I/O activity.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-159">可用記憶體的記憶體：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-159">Memory: Available Memory</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-160">這項分析會檢查是否總可用記憶體偏低 – 可用的 10%的警告和重大在可用的 5%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-160">This analysis checks whether the total available memory is low – Warning at 10 percent available and Critical at 5 percent available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-161">警告也會收到警示，每小時 10 MB 的遞減趨勢偵測到時，可指出潛在的即將進行的記憶體不足。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-161">A warning is also alerted when a decreasing trend of 10 MB’s per hour is detected, which can indicate a potential upcoming memory condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-162">實體記憶體不足可能會造成更高特殊權限的模式 CPU 和系統的延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-162">Low physical memory can cause increased privileged mode CPU and system delays.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-163">如需詳細資訊，請參閱可用 MemoryAnalysis 本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-163">For more information, refer to Available MemoryAnalysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-164">記憶體： 可用系統分頁表項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-164">Memory: Free System Page Table Entries</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-165">Free System Page Table Entries (PTE) 是由系統目前未使用的分頁表項目數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-165">Free System Page Table Entries (PTE’s) are the number of page table entries not currently used by the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-166">這項分析會判斷系統是否已執行超出 PTE 的方式是檢查是否有少於 5000 可用 PTE 的警告是否少於 10,000 可用 PTE 的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-166">This analysis determines whether the system is running out of PTE’s by checking whether there are fewer than 5,000 free PTE’s with a Warning if there are fewer than 10,000 free PTE’s.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-167">缺乏足夠 PTE 可能會導致整個系統停止回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-167">Lack of enough PTE’s can result in systemwide hangs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-168">也請注意，/3GB 參數將會大幅降低可用 PTE 數量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-168">Also note that the /3GB switch will lower the amount of free PTE’s significantly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-169">如需詳細資訊，請參閱可用系統分頁資料表項目分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-169">For more information, refer to Free System Page Table Entries Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-170">記憶體： 記憶體流失偵測</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-170">Memory: Memory Leak Detection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-171">這項分析會判斷是否的任何程序正在耗用大量系統的記憶體和處理程序是否在經過一段時間的記憶體耗用量增加。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-171">This analysis determines whether any of the processes are consuming a large amount of the system's memory and whether the process is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-172">處理序耗用是記憶體的正常的只要在處理序傳回回系統的記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-172">A process consuming large portions of memory is fine as long as the process returns the memory back to the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-173">尋找增加圖表中的趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-173">Look for increasing trends in the chart.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-174">遞增趨勢上很長一段時間可能表示記憶體流失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-174">An increasing trend over a long period of time could indicate a memory leak.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-175">「 私用位元組 」 是目前的大小，以位元組為單位，此處理序已配置的記憶體不能與其他處理序共用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-175">“Private Bytes” is the current size, in bytes, of memory that this process has allocated that cannot be shared with other processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-176">這項分析會檢查 10 MB 的每小時和 5 MB 的每小時增加的趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-176">This analysis checks for 10 MB’s per hour and 5 MB’s per hour increasing trends.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-177">您可以使用這項分析中與 PAL 中的可用記憶體分析相互關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-177">Use this analysis in correlation with the Available Memory analysis in PAL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-178">如需詳細資訊，請參閱記憶體流失偵測分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-178">For more information, refer to Memory Leak Detection Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-179">記憶體： 控制代碼遺漏偵測</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-179">Memory: Handle Leak Detection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-180">這項分析會檢查所有來判斷多少處理每個處理序已開啟，並懷疑來判斷是否控制代碼遺漏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-180">This analysis checks all of the processes to determine how many handles each has open and to determine whether a handle leak is suspected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-181">包含大量的控制代碼和/或積極增加的趨勢的程序可能表示有控制代碼流失，通常會導致記憶體流失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-181">A process with a large number of handles and/or an aggressive upward trend could indicate a handle leak, which typically results in a memory leak.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-182">此程序目前開啟的控制代碼總數會等於這個處理序中的每個執行緒目前開啟的控制代碼總和。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-182">The total number of handles currently open by this process is equal to the sum of the handles currently open by each thread in this process.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-183">參考： 偵錯診斷工具 v1.1，在 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-183">Reference:  Debug Diagnostic Tool v1.1 at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-184">記憶體： 記憶體 Pages Input/sec</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-184">Memory: Memory Pages Input/sec</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-185">「 Pages Input/sec"是從磁碟為解決硬體分頁錯誤而讀取分頁的速率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-185">“Pages Input/sec” is the rate at which pages are read from disk to resolve hard page faults.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-186">處理程序是指不在其工作集或其他位置中的實體記憶體，因而必須從磁碟擷取的虛擬記憶體分頁時，就會發生硬體分頁錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-186">Hard page faults occur when a process refers to a page in virtual memory that is not in its working set or elsewhere in physical memory, and must be retrieved from disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-187">這項分析會檢查是否有 10 個以上每秒的分頁檔案讀取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-187">This analysis checks whether there are more than 10 page file reads per second.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-188">Memory: Memory Pages/sec</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-188">Memory: Memory Pages/sec</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-189">這項分析會檢查是否"Pages/sec"很高 （超過 1,000 個）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-189">This analysis checks to see whether the “Pages/sec” is high (above 1,000).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-190">如果高，然後系統可能記憶體不足嘗試將頁面上的記憶體到磁碟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-190">If it is high, then the system is likely running out of memory by trying to page the memory to the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-191">「 頁/sec"是在讀取或寫入為解決硬體分頁錯誤而對磁碟頁面的速率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-191">“Pages/sec” is the rate at which pages are read from or written to disk to resolve hard page faults.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-192">這個計數器是導致整個系統延遲的錯誤種類的主要指示器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-192">This counter is a primary indicator of the kinds of faults that cause systemwide delays.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-193">您可以使用這項分析中可用的記憶體分析與 PAL 中的記憶體流失偵測分析相互關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-193">Use this analysis in correlation with Available Memory analysis and Memory Leak Detection analysis in PAL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-194">如果所有這些分析會擲回警示，在相同的時間，然後這可能表示系統用完記憶體，並根據推測的處理程序牽涉到 PAL 中的記憶體流失偵測分析中所述步驟分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-194">If all of these analyses are throwing alerts at the same time, then this may indicate the system is running out of memory and the suspected processes involved and follow analysis steps mentioned in the Memory Leak Detection analysis in PAL.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-195">如需詳細資訊，請參閱本主題中的記憶體 Pages/sec 分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-195">For more information, refer to Memory Pages/sec Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-196">記憶體： 記憶體系統快取常駐位元組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-196">Memory: Memory System Cache Resident Bytes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-197">「 系統快取常駐位元組 」 是大小，以位元組為單位的檔案系統快取中的可分頁作業系統程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-197">“System Cache Resident Bytes” is the size, in bytes, of the pageable operating system code in the file system cache.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-198">此值只包含目前實體頁面，而且不包含任何非目前駐留的虛擬記憶體分頁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-198">This value includes only current physical pages and does not include any virtual memory pages not currently resident.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-199">這個值是元件的 「 記憶體\\\System 程式碼常駐位元組 」 代表所有目前正在實體記憶體的可分頁作業系統程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-199">This value is a component of “Memory\\\System Code Resident Bytes” which represents all pageable operating system code that is currently in physical memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-200">這個計數器會顯示最後觀察到的值它不是平均值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-200">This counter displays the last observed value only; it is not an average.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-201">這項分析會檢查每小時 10 MB 的遞增趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-201">This analysis checks for an increasing trend of 10 MB’s per hour.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-202">在負載下，伺服器可能會以快取的 I/O 活動，例如磁碟使用的系統快取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-202">Under load, a server might use the system cache in order to cache I/O activity such as disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-203">用於相互關聯處理序 IO Data Operations/sec 與其他處理序 IO 作業數/秒 PAL 中的分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-203">Use in correlation with Process IO Data Operations/sec and Process IO Other Operations/sec analyses in PAL.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-204">參考： 檔案快取效能和調整在 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106786](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106786)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-204">Reference: File Cache Performance and Tuning at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106786](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106786)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-205">記憶體： 集區未分頁位元組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-205">Memory: Pool Non Paged Bytes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-206">"Pool Nonpaged 的 Bytes 」 是以位元組為單位的非分頁集區，不能寫入的物件系統記憶體區域的大小，磁碟、 但只要已配置就必須保留在實體記憶體中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-206">“Pool Nonpaged Bytes” is the size, in bytes, of the non-paged pool, an area of system memory for objects that cannot be written to disk, but must remain in physical memory as long as they are allocated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-207">這項分析會檢查以查看系統即將推出，接近 最大的集區未分頁記憶體大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-207">This analysis checks to see whether the system is coming close to the maximum pool non paged memory size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-208">它會透過評估下列因素納入考量的集區大小/3 GB、 實體記憶體大小，以及 32 位元/64 位元，然後判斷值是否大於估計的集區大小的 60%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-208">It does this by estimating the pool sizes taking into consideration /3GB, physical memory size, and 32-bit/64-bit, then determining whether the value is higher than 60 percent of the estimated pool size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-209">如果系統變成接近最大大小，系統可能會導致系統寬的停止回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-209">If the system becomes close to the maximum size, then the system could experience system wide hangs.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-210">Boot.ini 檔案中的 3 GB 交換器選項會大幅降低此記憶體集區的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-210">The /3GB switch option in the boot.ini file significantly reduces the size of this memory pool.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-211">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 Pool Non-Paged 位元組分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-211">For more information, refer to Pool Non-Paged Bytes Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-212">記憶體： 集區分頁位元組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-212">Memory: Pool Paged Bytes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-213">這項分析會檢查以查看系統即將推出，接近 最大的集區的分頁記憶體大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-213">This analysis checks to see whether the system is coming close to the maximum pool paged memory size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-214">它會透過評估下列因素納入考量的集區大小/3 GB、 實體記憶體大小，以及 32 位元/64 位元，然後判斷值是否大於估計的集區大小的 60%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-214">It does this by estimating the pool sizes taking into consideration /3GB, physical memory size, and 32-bit/64-bit, then determining whether the value is higher than 60 percent of the estimated pool size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-215">如果系統變成接近最大大小，系統可能會導致系統寬的停止回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-215">If the system becomes close to the maximum size, then the system could experience system wide hangs.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-216">Boot.ini 檔案中的 3 GB 交換器選項會大幅降低此記憶體集區的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-216">The /3GB switch option in the boot.ini file significantly reduces the size of this memory pool.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-217">如需詳細資訊，請參閱集區的分頁位元組分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-217">For more information, refer to Pool Paged Bytes Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-218">記憶體： 處理序執行緒計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-218">Memory: Process Thread Count</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-219">這項分析會檢查所有的處理序，來決定處理程序是否有超過 500 個執行緒，以及如果 50 執行緒每小時增加的執行緒數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-219">This analysis checks all of the processes to determine whether a process has more than 500 threads and if the number of threads is increasing by 50 threads per hour.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-220">大量執行緒和/或積極增加的趨勢的處理序可能表示執行緒遺漏通常會導致記憶體遺漏或高內容切換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-220">A process with a large number of threads and/or an aggressive upward trend could indicate a thread leak which typically results in either a memory leak or high context switching.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-221">高內容切換，會導致高特殊權限模式 CPU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-221">High context switching will result in high privileged mode CPU.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-222">記憶體： 處理程序工作組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-222">Memory: Process Working Set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-223">「 工作集 」 是目前的大小，以位元組為單位的工作集，此程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-223">“Working Set” is the current size, in bytes, of the working set of this process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-224">工作集是由程序中執行緒最近觸及的記憶體分頁的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-224">The working set is the set of memory pages touched recently by the threads in the process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-225">如果電腦中的可用記憶體超過閾值，頁面會留在程序的工作集，即使他們沒有使用中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-225">If free memory in the computer is above a threshold, pages are left in the working set of a process even if they are not in use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-226">當可用記憶體低於臨界值時，會從工作集修剪頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-226">When free memory falls below a threshold, pages are trimmed from working sets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-227">若您需要這些然後再將其寫回工作集退出主記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-227">If they are needed they will then be soft-faulted back into the working set before leaving main memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-228">這項分析會檢查遞增趨勢的 10 MB 以上每個處理程序中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-228">This analysis checks for an increasing trend of 10 MB’s or more in each of the processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-229">在相互關聯使用 PAL 中的可用記憶體分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-229">Use in correlation with Available Memory analysis in PAL.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-230">參考： 偵測在記憶體瓶頸 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106787](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106787)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-230">Reference:  Detecting Memory Bottlenecks at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106787](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106787)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-231">網路： 網路輸出佇列長度分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-231">Network: Network Output Queue Length Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-232">這項分析會檢查網路介面卡上等候多少執行緒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-232">This analysis checks to see how many threads are waiting on the network adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-233">如果有很多執行緒正在等待網路介面卡，然後系統會可能讓網路飽和 I/O 由於網路延遲或網路頻寬。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-233">If a lot of threads are waiting on the network adapter, then the system is probably saturating the network I/O due to network latency or network bandwidth.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-234">「 輸出佇列長度 」 （以封包） 的輸出封包佇列長度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-234">“Output Queue Length” is the length of the output packet queue (in packets).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-235">延遲會指出如果這是長度大於二，並且應該找到並盡快解決瓶頸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-235">Delays are indicated if this is longer than two, and the bottleneck should be found and eliminated, if possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-236">網路輸出佇列的一般原因包括大量的小型網路要求和網路延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-236">Typical causes of network output queuing include high numbers of small network requests and network latency.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-237">網路： 網路使用率分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-237">Network: Network Utilization Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-238">「 Bytes Total/sec"是在傳送及接收每個網路介面卡，包括框架字元位元組的速率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-238">“Bytes Total/sec” is the rate at which bytes are sent and received over each network adapter, including framing characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-239">"Network Interface\Bytes Received/sec"是"Network Interface\Bytes Received/sec"和"Network Interface\Bytes Sent/sec"的總和。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-239">“Network Interface\Bytes Received/sec” is a sum of “Network Interface\Bytes Received/sec” and “Network Interface\Bytes Sent/sec”.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-240">此計數器可協助您了解在您的網路介面卡的流量是否已飽和，以及您是否需要新增另一個網路介面卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-240">This counter helps you know whether the traffic at your network adapter is saturated and whether you need to add another network adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-241">您可以識別問題的速度取決於類型有以及您是否與其他應用程式共用頻寬的網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-241">How quickly you can identify a problem depends on the type of network you have as well as whether you share bandwidth with other applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-242">這項分析會將"Bytes Total/sec"轉換成位元，並比較計算網路使用率的網路介面卡的目前頻寬。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-242">This analysis converts “Bytes Total/sec” to bits and compares it to the current bandwidth of the network adapter to calculate network utilization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-243">接下來，它會檢查使用量超過 50%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-243">Next, it checks for utilization above 50 percent.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-244">參考： 測量在.NET 應用程式效能 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-244">Reference:  Measuring .NET Application Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-245">分頁檔： 分頁檔案使用量百分比和 %使用率正達尖峰</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-245">Paging File: Paging File % Usage and % Usage Peak</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-246">以百分比表示的使用中的頁面檔案執行個體數量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-246">The amount of the page file instance in use in percent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-247">另請參閱 「 處理程序\\\Page File Bytes"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-247">See also “Process\\\Page File Bytes”.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-248">這項分析會檢查是否使用的百分比大於 70%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-248">This analysis checks whether the percentage of usage is greater than 70 percent.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-249">處理器： 處理器使用率分析和處理序過度佔用處理器使用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-249">Processor: Processor Utilization Analysis and Excessive Processor Use by Processes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-250">此計數器是處理器活動的主要指示器，並顯示在取樣間隔期間觀察到的忙碌時間平均百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-250">This counter is the primary indicator of processor activity and displays the average percentage of busy time observed during the sample interval.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-251">其計算方式是監視該服務處於非使用中的時間，並從 100%減去該值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-251">It is calculated by monitoring the time that the service is inactive and subtracting that value from 100 percent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-252">這項分析會檢查使用量大於每個處理器上的 60%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-252">This analysis checks for utilization greater than 60 percent on each processor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-253">如果是的話，判斷它是否高使用者模式 CPU 或高特殊權限的模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-253">If so, determine whether it is high user mode CPU or high privileged mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-254">如果懷疑 CPU 高特殊權限的模式，則會看到在 PAL 中的特殊權限模式 CPU 分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-254">If high privileged mode CPU is suspected, then see the Privileged Mode CPU analysis in PAL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-255">如果懷疑有使用者模式處理器瓶頸，請考慮使用處理程序的程式碼剖析工具分析造成高 CPU 耗用率的函式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-255">If a user-mode processor bottleneck is suspected, then consider using a process profiler to analyze the functions causing the high CPU consumption.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-256">處理器： 處理器佇列長度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-256">Processor: Processor Queue Length</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-257">這項分析會判斷是否平均處理器佇列長度會超過處理器的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-257">This analysis determines whether the average processor queue length exceeds the number of processors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-258">如果是的話，這可能表示發生處理器瓶頸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-258">If so, then this could indicate a processor bottleneck.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-259">使用這項分析中使用特殊權限模式 CPU 分析和過多的處理器使用 PAL 中的程序分析的相互關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-259">Use this analysis in correlation with Privileged Mode CPU analysis and Excessive Processor Use by Process analysis in PAL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-260">如需詳細資訊，請參閱處理器佇列長度分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-260">For detailed information, refer to Processor Queue Length Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-261">處理器： 特殊權限的模式 CPU 分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-261">Processor:  Privileged Mode CPU Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-262">此計數器表示執行緒在特權模式下執行的時間的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-262">This counter indicates the percentage of time a thread runs in privileged mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-263">當您的應用程式呼叫作業系統函式 （例如來執行檔案或網路 I/O，或配置記憶體） 時，這些作業系統函式會執行特殊權限模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-263">When your application calls operating system functions (for example to perform file or network I/O or to allocate memory), these operating system functions are executed in privileged mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-264">這項分析會檢查是否有權限的模式 CPU 耗用超過 30%的總 CPU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-264">This analysis checks to see whether privileged mode CPU is consuming more than 30 percent of total CPU.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-265">如果，則 CPU 耗用量可能是另一個以外的處理器，例如網路、 記憶體或磁碟 I/O 瓶頸所造成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-265">If so, then the CPU consumption is likely caused by another bottleneck other than the processor such as network, memory, or disk I/O.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-266">用於相互關聯的處理器: %Interrupt Time 及處理器： 高內容切換在 PAL 中的分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-266">Use in correlation with Processor:  % Interrupt Time and Processor:  High Context Switching analyses in PAL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-267">如需詳細資訊，請參閱特殊權限模式 CPU 分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-267">For more information, refer to Privileged Mode CPU Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-268">處理器： 中斷時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-268">Processor: Interrupt Time</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-269">"%Interrupt Time 是處理器花費在接收與處理硬體插斷取樣間隔期間的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-269">“% Interrupt Time” is the time the processor spends receiving and servicing hardware interrupts during sample intervals.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-270">這個值是產生插斷，例如系統時鐘、 滑鼠、 磁碟驅動程式、 資料通訊線路、 網路介面卡及其他週邊裝置的裝置活動的間接指示器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-270">This value is an indirect indicator of the activity of devices that generate interrupts, such as the system clock, the mouse, disk drivers, data communication lines, network interface cards and other peripheral devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-271">在已完成工作，或需要注意時，這些裝置通常插斷處理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-271">These devices normally interrupt the processor when they have completed a task or require attention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-272">在插斷期間會暫停執行一般執行緒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-272">Normal thread execution is suspended during interrupts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-273">大多數的系統時鐘會插斷處理器每隔 10 毫秒，建立中斷活動的背景。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-273">Most system clocks interrupt the processor every 10 milliseconds, creating a background of interrupt activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-274">在此計數器指出可能硬體問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-274">A dramatic increase in this counter indicates potential hardware problems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-275">這項分析會檢查 「 插斷時間百分比 」 大於百分之 30。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-275">This analysis checks for “% Interrupt Time” greater than 30 percent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-276">如果發生這種情況，請考慮更新此警示的相互關聯的硬體的裝置驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-276">If this occurs, then consider updating devices drivers for hardware that correlates to this alert.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-277">參考： 測量在.NET 應用程式效能 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-277">Reference: Measuring .NET Application Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-278">處理器： 高內容切換</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-278">Processor:  High Context Switching</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-279">當高優先順序的執行緒優先執行較低優先順序的執行緒目前正在執行或高優先權執行緒會封鎖，就會發生內容切換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-279">A context switch happens when a higher priority thread preempts a lower priority thread that is currently running or when a high priority thread blocks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-280">多執行緒共用相同的優先權層級，就會發生內容切換的高層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-280">High levels of context switching can occur when many threads share the same priority level.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-281">這通常表示太多執行緒會在系統上處理器的競爭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-281">This often indicates that too many threads are competing for the processors on the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-282">一般而言，內容切換率小於每個處理器每秒 5000 就不值得耽心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-282">As a general rule, context switching rates of less than 5,000 per second per processor are not worth worrying about.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-283">如果內容切換率超過 15,000 每個處理器每秒，就將條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-283">If context switching rates exceed 15,000 per second per processor, then there is a constraint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-284">如需詳細資訊，請參閱高內容切換分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-284">For more information, refer to High Context Switching Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-285">Microsof BizTalk Server: BizTalk 凍結協調流程</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-285">Microsof BizTalk Server: BizTalk Dehydrating Orchestrations</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-286">當許多長時間執行商務程序在相同的時間執行時，記憶體和效能問題可能會進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-286">When many long-running business processes are running at the same time, memory and performance issues are possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-287">協調流程引擎透過「凍結」和「解除凍結」協調流程執行個體來解決這些問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-287">The orchestration engine addresses these issues by "dehydrating" and "rehydrating" orchestration instances.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-288">凍結是將協調流程狀態序列化到 SQL Server 資料庫中的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-288">Dehydration is the process of serializing the state of an orchestration into a SQL Server database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-289">解除凍結是此程序的反向︰ 還原序列化的協調流程從資料庫上次執行狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-289">Rehydration is the reverse of this process: deserializing the last running state of an orchestration from the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-290">凍結是藉由減少必須一次在記憶體中產生的協調流程數目，來將系統資源的使用降至最低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-290">Dehydration is used to minimize the use of system resources by reducing the number of orchestrations that have to be instantiated in memory at one time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-291">因此，dehyrations 儲存記憶體耗用量，但可執行相當耗費資源的作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-291">Therefore, dehyrations save memory consumption, but are relatively expensive operations to perform.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-292">這項分析會檢查 dehydrations 10 倍或更多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-292">This analysis checks for dehydrations of 10 or more.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-293">如果是這樣，[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]可能記憶體不足 （虛擬或實體），請執行高效能的協調流程數等待在訊息上或凍結設定不正確。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-293">If so, [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] may be running out of memory (either virtual or physical), a high number of orchestrations are waiting on messages, or the dehydration settings are not set properly.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-294">參考： 協調流程凍結和解除凍結在  [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-294">Reference:  Orchestration Dehydration and Rehydration at  [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-295">Microsoft BizTalk Server: BizTalk 高資料庫工作階段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-295">Microsoft BizTalk Server:  BizTalk High Database Sessions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-296">此計數器有兩個可能的值： normal (0) 或超過閾值 (1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-296">This counter has two possible values: normal (0) or exceeded (1).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-297">這項分析會檢查值為 1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-297">This analysis checks for a value of 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-298">如果是這樣，BizTalk 已超過允許的資料庫工作階段數目的臨界值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-298">If so, BizTalk has exceeded the threshold of the number of database sessions permitted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-299">這個值是由 「 每一 CPU 的資料庫連線 」 中的值的 BizTalk 主控件節流設定所控制的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-299">This value is controlled by the “Database connection per CPU” value in the BizTalk Host Throttling settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-300">「 資料庫每一 CPU 的連線 」 為並行資料庫工作階段數目上限 （每一 CPU) 節流開始前允許。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-300">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-301">您可以使用 biztalk： 訊息代理程式的效能物件類別下的資料庫工作階段效能計數器來監視作用中資料庫連線數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-301">You can monitor the number of active Database connections by using the Database session performance counter under the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-302">此參數只會影響輸出訊息節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-302">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-303">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk 高資料庫工作階段分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-303">For more information, refer to BizTalk High Database Sessions Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-304">Microsoft BizTalk Server: BizTalk 高資料庫大小</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-304">Microsoft BizTalk Server: BizTalk High Database Size</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-305">此計數器將設定為值 1，如果其中一個列出的資料庫臨界值中的訊息計數的條件發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-305">This counter will be set to a value of 1 if either of the conditions listed for the message count in database threshold occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-306">根據預設主機訊息資料庫節流閾值中的計數是設定為 50000，將會觸發節流狀況，在下列情況下的值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-306">By default the host message count in database throttling threshold is set to a value of 50,000, which will trigger a throttling condition under the following circumstances:</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-307">訊息發佈的工作、 狀態和擱置的佇列訂閱的主控件的主控件執行個體-總數超過 50,000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-307">-   The total number of messages published by the host instance to the work, state, and suspended queues of the subscribing hosts exceeds 50,000.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-308">-多工緩衝處理表格或追蹤資料表中的訊息數目超過 500,000 訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-308">-   The number of messages in the spool table or the tracking table exceeds 500,000 messages.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-309">如果發生這種情況，請考慮採取的動作，將會減少在資料庫中的訊息數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-309">If this occurs, then consider a course of action that will reduce the number of messages in the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-310">例如，請在 SQL Server 工作[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]正在執行不會發生錯誤，而且使用中的 [群組中樞] 頁面[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]管理主控台來判斷訊息增多是否因大量擱置的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-310">For example, ensure the SQL Server jobs in [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] are running without error and use the Group Hub page in the [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] Administration console to determine whether message build up is caused by large numbers of suspended messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-311">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk 高資料庫大小分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-311">For more information, refer to BizTalk High Database Size Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-312">Microsoft BizTalk Server: BizTalk 高內含式訊息計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-312">Microsoft BizTalk Server:  BizTalk High In-Process Message Count</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-313">這項分析會檢查以判斷是否發生這種節流高內含式訊息計數計數器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-313">This analysis checks the High In-Process Message Count counter to determine whether this kind of throttling is occurring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-314">如果是的話，請考慮調整"訊息每一 CPU 的內含式 」 設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-314">If so, consider adjusting the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-315">此參數只會影響輸出訊息節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-315">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-316">在停用以每一 CPU 的內含式訊息數目為基礎的節流"訊息每一 CPU 的內含式 」 設定中輸入值為 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-316">Enter a value of 0 in the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting to disable throttling based on the number of in-process messages per CPU.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-317">「 內含式訊息每一 CPU 」 設定的預設值是 1000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-317">The default value for the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting is 1,000.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-318">請注意，此值也可能會影響低度延遲的訊息和 （或） BizTalk 資源的效率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-318">Note that modifying this value can also have an impact on low latency of messages and/or the efficiency of BizTalk resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-319">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk 高內含式訊息計數分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-319">For more information, refer to BizTalk High In-Process Message Count Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-344">Microsoft BizTalk Server: BizTalk 高執行緒計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-344">Microsoft BizTalk Server:  BizTalk High Thread Count</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-345">[每一 CPU 的執行緒] 是在主機處理程序包括使用配接器之執行緒的執行緒總數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-345">“Threads Per CPU” is the total number of threads in the host process including threads used by adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-346">如果超過此閾值，[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]會嘗試減少 EPM 執行緒集區和訊息代理程式 」 執行緒集區的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-346">If this threshold is exceeded, [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] will try to reduce the size of the EPM thread pool and message agent thread pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-347">在高負載可能導致建立大量執行緒的情況時，應啟用以執行緒為基礎的節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-347">Thread based throttling should be enabled in scenarios where high load can lead to the creation of a large number of threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-348">此參數會同時影響輸入和輸出節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-348">This parameter affects both inbound and outbound throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-349">執行緒為基礎的節流預設為停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-349">Thread based throttling is disabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-350">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk 高執行緒計數分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-350">For more information, refer to BizTalk High Thread Count Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|

data-ttu-id="9fc74-363">通常，因訊息有問題而擱置的執行個體不會繼續執行，而且必須修正訊息本身，並重新提交至[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-363">Often, suspended instances due to a message problem are not resumable, and the message itself must be fixed and resubmitted to the [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] system.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-364">擱置的訊息佇列是包含的錯誤或失敗期間發生未處理的工作項目。</span><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-365">訊息擱置佇列會儲存訊息直到修正和重新處理或是刪除後為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-365">A suspended queue stores the messages until they can be corrected and reprocessed, or deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-366">這項分析會檢查擱置的任何的訊息項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-366">This analysis checks for any occurrence of suspended messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-367">增加的趨勢可能表示嚴重處理錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-367">An increasing trend could indicate severe processing errors.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-368">參考： BizTalk Server 2004： 監視和疑難排解於 |<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-369">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 閒置協調流程</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-369">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Idle Orchestrations</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-370">目前由主控件執行個體裝載而閒置的協調流程執行個體數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-370">Number of idle orchestration instances currently hosted by the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-371">此計數器是指不進行進度，但不是可凍結的協調流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-371">This counter refers to orchestrations that are not making progress but are not dehydratable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-372">可能會發生這種情況下，協調流程遭到封鎖時，等待接收，接聽或不可部分完成的交易的延遲時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-372">This situation can occur when the orchestration is blocked, waiting for a receive, listen, or delay in an atomic transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-373">如果大量的非可凍結的協調流程會累積，BizTalk 可能用盡記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-373">If a large number of non-dehydratable orchestrations accumulate, then BizTalk may run out of memory.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-374">凍結是將協調流程狀態序列化到 SQL Server 資料庫中的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-374">Dehydration is the process of serializing the state of an orchestration into a SQL Server database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-375">解除凍結是此程序的反向︰ 還原序列化的協調流程從資料庫上次執行狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-375">Rehydration is the reverse of this process: deserializing the last running state of an orchestration from the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-376">凍結是藉由減少必須一次在記憶體中產生的協調流程數目，來將系統資源的使用降至最低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-376">Dehydration is used to minimize the use of system resources by reducing the number of orchestrations that have to be instantiated in memory at one time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-377">引擎會儲存狀態以凍結執行個體，並釋出執行個體所需的記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-377">The engine dehydrates the instance by saving the state, and frees up the memory required by the instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-378">透過凍結休眠的協調流程執行個體，引擎就可以讓大量的長時間執行之商務程序在相同電腦上同時執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-378">By dehydrating dormant orchestration instances, the engine makes it possible for a large number of long-running business processes to run concurrently on the same computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-379">這項分析會檢查遞增趨勢的一個每小時的閒置協調流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-379">This analysis checks for an increasing trend of one idle orchestration per hour.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-380">參考： 協調流程凍結和解除凍結在  [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-380">Reference: Orchestration Dehydration and Rehydration at |<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-381">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 輸入延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-381">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Inbound Latency</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-382">平均延遲 （毫秒），傳訊引擎收到文件從配接器之前發佈到 MessageBox 的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-382">Average latency in milliseconds from when the messaging engine receives a document from the adapter until the time it is published to the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-383">降低延遲很重要的 BizTalk 中，某些使用者因此追蹤時間文件花費輸入配接器中很重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-383">Reducing latency is important to some users of BizTalk, therefore tracking how much time documents spend in the inbound adapter is important.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-384">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk 輸入延遲分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-384">For more information, refer to BizTalk Inbound Latency Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-385">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 訊息傳遞延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-385">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Message Delivery Delay</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-386">這是加諸於 （適用於訊息傳遞進行節流處理） 每個訊息傳遞批次的目前延遲 （毫秒） （毫秒）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-386">This is the current delay in milliseconds (ms) imposed on each message delivery batch (applicable if the message delivery is being throttled).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-387">節流就而言，在發行或處理訊息，根據訊息是傳入或傳出時套用延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-387">In regards to throttling, a delay is applied in the publishing or processing of the message, depending on whether the message is inbound or outbound.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-388">延遲期間為節流狀況的嚴重性成正比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-388">The delay period is proportional to the severity of the throttling condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-389">較高的嚴重性節流狀況將會起始與較低的嚴重性節流狀況更長的節流期間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-389">Higher severity throttling conditions will initiate a longer throttling period than lower severity throttling conditions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-390">透過狀況變更時的節流機制，這個延遲期間可在特定範圍內上下調整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-390">This delay period is adjusted up and down within certain ranges by the throttling mechanism as conditions change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-391">目前的延遲期間會公開透過訊息傳遞延遲 （毫秒） 」 和 「 訊息發佈延遲 （毫秒） 效能計數器與 biztalk： 訊息代理程式的效能物件類別相關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-391">The current delay period is exposed through the message delivery delay (ms) and the message publishing delay (ms) performance counters associated with the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-392">這項分析會檢查訊息傳遞延遲大於 5 秒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-392">This analysis checks for a message delivery delay of greater than 5 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-393">由於高負載過重節流，可能表示長訊息傳遞延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-393">Long message delivery delays may indicate heavy throttling due to high load.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-394">參考： |<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-410">BizTalk Server: BizTalk MessageBox 資料庫連線失敗</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-410">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk MessageBox Database Connection Failures</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-411">此效能計數器是資料庫連線嘗試的主控件執行個體啟動後失敗的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-411">This performance counter is the number of attempted database connections that failed since the host instance started.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-412">如果裝載 BizTalk 資料庫的 SQL Server 服務因故無法使用，資料庫叢集資源從作用中的電腦傳輸到被動電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-412">If the SQL Server service hosting the BizTalk databases becomes unavailable for any reason, the database cluster transfers resources from the active computer to the passive computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-413">在容錯移轉過程中，[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]服務執行個體發生資料庫連線失敗，並自動重新啟動以重新連接到資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-413">During this failover process, the [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] service instances experience database connection failures and automatically restart to reconnect to the databases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-414">正在運作的資料庫電腦 (先前為被動電腦) 會在容錯移轉期間獲得資源後，開始處理資料庫連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-414">The functioning database computer (previously the passive computer) begins processing the database connections after assuming the resources during failover.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-415">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk MessageBox 資料庫連線失敗分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-415">For more information, refer to BizTalk MessageBox Database Connection Failures Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-428">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 協調流程已暫停/秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-428">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Orchestration Suspended/second</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-429">擱置的訊息是訊息或協調流程的執行個體，[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]已停止處理因錯誤而在系統或訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-429">A suspended message is an instance of a message or orchestration that [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] has stopped processing due to an error in the system or the message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-430">一般來說，因系統錯誤而擱置的執行個體會在系統問題獲得解決後繼續。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-430">Generally, suspended instances caused by system errors are resumable upon resolution of the system issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-431">通常，因訊息有問題而擱置的執行個體不會繼續執行，而且必須修正訊息本身，並重新提交至[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-431">Often, suspended instances due to a message problem are not resumable, and the message itself must be fixed and resubmitted to the [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-432">這項分析會檢查任何擱置的訊息/協調流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-432">This analysis checks for any suspended messages/orchestrations.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-433">參考： BizTalk Server 2004： 監視和疑難排解於 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108771](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108771)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-433">Reference:  BizTalk Server 2004: Monitoring and Troubleshooting at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108771](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108771)</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-448">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 配接器輸出延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-448">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Outbound Adapter Latency</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-449">這是平均延遲的秒數從當配接器取得傳訊引擎從配接器傳送的時間之前的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-449">This is the average latency in seconds from when the adapter gets a document from the messaging engine until the time it is sent by the adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-450">請參閱顯示 BizTalk 輸入延遲分析中測量延遲是方式，本主題中的圖表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-450">Refer to the chart showing how latency is measured in BizTalk Inbound Latency Analysis in this topic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-451">假設在低延遲的環境，這項分析會檢查延遲大於 5 秒的輸出配接器中的平均。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-451">Assuming a low latency environment, this analysis checks for latency in the outbound adapter of greater than 5 seconds on average.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-452">這可能表示之傳輸的輸出配接器在此主控件執行個體中的訊息處理延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-452">This may indicate a processing delay in the transport of messages through outbound adapters in this host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-453">如果多個輸出配接器存在於此主控件執行個體，請考慮將它們分割到他們自己的主機，來判斷哪些輸出配接器都有高延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-453">If multiple outbound adapters exist in this host instance, then consider separating them into their own hosts to determine which outbound adapter has high latency.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-454">參考：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-454">References:</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-455">-要求/回應訊息在 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155288](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155288)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-455">-   Request/Response Messaging at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155288](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155288)</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-456">BizTalk Server 2006： 使用 BizTalk Server 2006: Scalability Case Study Using the SOAP Adapter in BizTalk Server 2006 at |<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-459">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 暫止訊息數目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-459">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Pending Messages</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-460">接收到 MessageBox 收到尚未認可的訊息數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-460">The number of received messages that have not been acknowledged as received to the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-461">暫止訊息數目會有已提取到記憶體，並傳遞至 XLANG 協調流程中，但尚未已處理訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-461">Pending messages are messages that have been pulled into memory and delivered to the XLANG orchestration, but have not yet been processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-462">這種情況下沒有遺失資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-462">This circumstance has nothing to do with data loss.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-463">將訊息傳遞到協調流程是多步驟程序，只是位在資料庫中的多工緩衝處理資料表中的訊息執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-463">Delivering a message to an orchestration is a multi-step process and is simply an instance of the message residing in the spool table in the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-464">這些暫止訊息計數為內含式訊息。因此，需要大量的記憶體中可能會導致記憶體節流系統上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-464">These pending messages count as in-process messages; therefore, having a large number of them in memory could cause memory throttling on the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-465">調整 [內部訊息佇列大小] 設定可以協助控制的暫止訊息數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-465">Adjusting the Internal Message Queue Size setting could help with controlling the number of pending messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-466">每個 CPU 的內含式訊息設定將會影響當節流會叫用時就會發生大量的暫止訊息數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-466">The In-Process Messages Per CPU setting has an impact on when throttling will invoke when a high number of pending messages occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-467">在 BizTalk 管理主控台的主機內容中找到這些設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-467">These setting are found in the Host properties in the BizTalk Administration Console.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-468">這項分析會檢查只有此計數器會顯示統計資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-468">This analysis checks only shows statistics for this counter.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-469">參考： 在協調流程引擎效能計數器 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155290](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155290)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-469">Reference: Orchestration Engine Performance Counters at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155290](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155290)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-470">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 持續點/秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-470">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Persistence Points/second</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-471">平均每秒保存的協調流程執行個體數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-471">Average number of orchestration instances persisted per second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-472">協調流程引擎會在不同點儲存執行中協調流程執行個體的狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-472">The orchestration engine saves the state of a running orchestration instance at various points.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-473">如果需要解除凍結協調流程執行個體、 從控制的關閉、 啟動或從非預期的關機復原，它會從上次保存點執行協調流程執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-473">If it needs to rehydrate the orchestration instance, start up from a controlled shutdown, or recover from an unexpected shutdown, it will run the orchestration instance from the last persistence point.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-474">以保存協調流程執行個體，所有物件直接或間接參考至您的協調流程的執行個體 （像是透過其他物件） 必須是可序列化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-474">In order to persist an orchestration instance, all object instances that your orchestration refers to directly or indirectly (as through other objects) must be serializable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-475">為訊息保存頻率 （資料需要保存的時間的數字） 增加，整體效能會降低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-475">As message-persistence frequency (the number of times that data needs to be persisted) increases, overall performance decreases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-476">作用中，每個持續點是來回存取資料庫，因此盡可能減少持續點的頻率避免或合併持續點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-476">In effect, each persistence point is a round trip to the database, so whenever possible reduce the frequency of persistence points by avoiding or consolidating persistence points.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-477">請參閱下方有關持續點發生時的參考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-477">See the references below for more information regarding when persistence points occur.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-478">這項分析會檢查有 10 個以上的持續點，每秒平均。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-478">This analysis checks for more than 10 persistence points per second on average.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-479">這是一般的起始點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-479">This is a general starting point.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-480">參考：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-480">References:</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-481">-在協調流程中的持續性 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155291](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155291)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-481">-   Persistence in Orchestrations at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155291](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155291)</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-482">持續性和在協調流程引擎 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155292](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155292)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-482">-   Persistence and the Orchestration Engine at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155292](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155292)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-483">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 私用位元組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-483">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Private Bytes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-484">這是主控件執行個體，其相當於"\Process （\*） \Private 位元組 」 效能計數器的配置私用記憶體 mb。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-484">This is the megabytes of allocated private memory for the host instance and comparable to the “\Process(\*)\Private Bytes” performance counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-485">這項分析會判斷是否任何主控件執行個體正在耗用龐大的系統記憶體和主控件執行個體是否持續一段時間的記憶體耗用量增加。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-485">This analysis determines whether any of the host instances are consuming a large size of the system's memory and whether the host instance is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-486">本主題，如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk 私用位元組分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-486">Refer to BizTalk Private Bytes Analysis in this topic for more information.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-487">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 多工緩衝處理表格大小</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-487">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Spool Table Size</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-488">MessageBox 多工緩衝處理表格包含系統中的每個訊息的記錄 (作用中或等候 「 記憶體回收 」)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-488">The MessageBox spool table contains a record for each message in the system (active or waiting to be "garbage collected").</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-489">監視此資料表中的資料列數目和增加系統負載提供簡單的方法來尋找最大持續輸送量時，每秒接收的訊息數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-489">Monitoring the number of rows in this table and the number of messages received per second while increasing system load provides an easy way to find the maximum sustainable throughput.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-490">只要增加輸入的負載可能是 1） 多工緩衝處理資料表會無止盡成長或 2） 的每個第二個富饒、 何者較早，和也就是您的最大持續輸送量收到的訊息數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-490">Simply increase the input load until either 1) the spool table starts to grow indefinitely or 2) the number of messages received per second plateaus, whichever comes first, and that is your maximum sustainable throughput.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-491">總而言之，不論其他指標，此量值可讓您快速輕鬆的方式，來評估您的系統正在既是否。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-491">In summary, regardless of other indicators, this measure will give you a quick and easy way to assess whether your system is being overdriven or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-492">當 BizTalk 多工緩衝處理表格大小增加的趨勢時，然後節流因為不平衡的訊息傳遞速率 （輸入的速率超過輸出速率） 或可能是由於資料庫大小而進行節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-492">When the BizTalk spool tables size is on an increasing trend, then throttling due to imbalanced message delivery rate (input rate exceeds output rate) or throttling due to Database size may occur.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-493">這項分析會檢查在 BizTalk 多工緩衝處理表格大小增加的趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-493">This analysis checks for an increasing trend in the BizTalk Spool Table Size.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-494">參考：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-494">References:</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-495">-了解 BizTalk Server 2004 SP1 輸送量和在容量 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108781](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108781)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-495">-   Understanding BizTalk Server 2004 SP1 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155293](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155293)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-496">-   Sustainable Load Test at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155293](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155293)</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-497">-建議測試引擎效能時
