Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155294](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155294)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-498">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 追蹤資料大小</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-498">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Tracking Data Size</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-499">當 BizTalk Server 處理您系統上的多資料時，BizTalk 追蹤資料庫 (BizTalkDTADb) 會繼續成長的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-499">As BizTalk Server processes more and more data on your system, the BizTalk Tracking database (BizTalkDTADb) continues to grow in size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-500">若未發現此成長現象將會降低系統效能，並且可能會在 Tracking Data Delivery Service (TDDS) 中產生錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-500">Unchecked growth decreases system performance and may generate errors in the Tracking Data Delivery Service (TDDS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-501">除了一般追蹤資料以外，追蹤的訊息也會累積在 MessageBox 資料庫，導致磁碟效能變差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-501">In addition to general tracking data, tracked messages can also accumulate in the MessageBox database, causing poor disk performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-502">這項分析會檢查遞增趨勢的多個 5 MB 的每小時追蹤中的資料大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-502">This analysis checks for an increasing trend of more than 5 MB’s per hour in the tracking data size.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-503">參考：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-503">Reference:</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-504">封存和清除 BizTalk 追蹤資料庫  [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=153816](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=153816)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-504">Archiving and Purging the BizTalk Tracking Database at  [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=153816](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=153816)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-505">BizTalk Server： 交易式範圍數 BizTalk 中止</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-505">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Transactional Scopes Aborted</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-506">這是長時間執行或不可部分完成範圍自從主控件執行個體啟動之後已中止的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-506">This is the number of long-running or atomic scopes that have been aborted since the host instance started.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-507">交易式範圍中止，則協調流程內的交易範圍內發生的失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-507">A transactional scope abort is a failure that occurs in a transaction scope within an orchestration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-508">請務必了解的範圍已順利完成，但是然後才可以復原，因為周圍的範圍決定 （因為在處理時稍後可能會發生的失敗） 而中止時，才叫用範圍的補償處理常式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-508">It is important to understand that the compensation handler of a scope is invoked only if the scope completed successfully, but then is required to be undone because a surrounding scope has decided to abort (due to failures that may occur later in the process).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-509">此外，「 自動 」 復原的狀態就會發生交易中止時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-509">Also, no "auto" rollback of state occurs in case of a transaction abort.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-510">您可以達到這個結果，以程式設計方式透過例外狀況和補償處理常式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-510">You can achieve this outcome programmatically through the exception and compensation handlers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-511">交易式範圍中止不應該通常發生在實際執行環境。因此，這項分析會檢查有任何已中止的交易式範圍的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-511">Transactional scope aborts should not normally occur in a production environment; therefore, this analysis checks for the occurrence of any transactional scopes aborted.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-512">參考：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-512">Reference:</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-513">在 BizTalk Server 2004 整個交易 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-513">Transactions Across BizTalk Server 2004 at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-514">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 交易式範圍補償</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-514">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Transactional Scopes Compensated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-515">補償可以視為邏輯工作，已成功提交回應某個錯誤狀況中復原。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-515">Compensation can be thought of as a logical undo of the work that has been successfully committed in response to some error condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-516">請務必了解的範圍已順利完成，但是然後才可以復原，因為周圍的範圍決定 （因為在處理時稍後可能會發生的失敗） 而中止時，才叫用範圍的補償處理常式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-516">It is important to understand that the compensation handler of a scope is invoked only if the scope completed successfully, but then is required to be undone because a surrounding scope has decided to abort (due to failures that may occur later in the process).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-517">此外，「 自動 」 復原的狀態就會發生交易中止時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-517">Also, no "auto" rollback of state occurs in case of a transaction abort.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-518">您可以透過例外狀況和補償處理常式，以程式設計方式來達成這點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-518">You can achieve this programmatically through the exception and compensation handlers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-519">交易式範圍的補償不應該通常發生在實際執行環境。因此，這項分析會檢查有任何已中止的交易式範圍的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-519">Transactional scope compensations should not normally occur in a production environment; therefore, this analysis checks for the occurrence of any transactional scopes aborted.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-520">在 BizTalk Server 2004 整個的參考： 交易 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-520">Reference: Transactions Across BizTalk Server 2004 at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-521">BizTalk Server: BizTalk Virtual Bytes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-521">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Virtual Bytes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-522">這是保留給主控件執行個體的虛擬記憶體 （mb）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-522">This is the megabytes reserved for virtual memory for the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-523">這項分析會決定是否任何主控件執行個體正在耗用大量系統的記憶體，以及是否在經過一段時間的記憶體耗用量增加主控件執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-523">This analysis determines whether any of the host instances are consuming a large amount of the system's memory and whether the host instance is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-524">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk 虛擬位元組分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-524">For more information, refer to BizTalk Virtual Bytes Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-525">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 訊息代理程式工作階段節流的資料庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-525">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-526">這是到 MessageBox，相較於其各自的 BizTalk 節流設定的開放式資料庫連接的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-526">This is the number of open database connections to the MessageBox compared to its respective BizTalk throttling setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-527">「 資料庫每一 CPU 的連線 」 為並行資料庫工作階段數目上限 （每一 CPU) 節流開始前允許。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-527">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-528">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk 訊息代理程式資料庫工作階段節流分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-528">For more information, refer to BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-529">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 訊息代理程式資料庫工作階段節流處理臨界值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-529">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling Threshold</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-530">這是到 MessageBox 的開放式資料庫連接數目的目前閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-530">This is the current threshold for the number of open database connections to the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-531">「 資料庫每一 CPU 的連線 」 為並行資料庫工作階段數目上限 （每一 CPU) 節流開始前允許。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-531">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-532">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk 訊息代理程式資料庫工作階段節流閾值分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-532">For more information, refer to BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling Threshold Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-533">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 訊息代理程式內含式訊息計數節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-533">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Message Agent In-process Message Count Throttling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-534">這是並行服務類別正在處理的訊息數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-534">This is the number of concurrent messages that the service class is processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-535">「 內含式訊息每一 CPU 」 中的設定主控件節流設定是傳遞至 「 結束點管理員 」 (EPM) 或 XLANG 尚未處理的訊息的數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-535">The “In-process messages per CPU” setting in the Host Throttling Settings is the maximum number of messages delivered to the End Point Manager (EPM) or XLANG that have not been processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-536">如需詳細資訊，請參閱本主題中 BizTalk 訊息代理程式內含式訊息計數節流分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-536">For more information, refer to BizTalk Message Agent In-process Message Count Throttling Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-537">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 訊息代理程式內含式訊息計數節流處理臨界值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-537">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Message Agent In-process Message Count Throttling Threshold</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-538">這是目前的服務類別正在處理的並行訊息數目的閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-538">This is the current threshold for the number of concurrent messages that the service class is processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-539">「 內含式訊息每一 CPU 」 中的設定主控件節流設定是傳遞至 「 結束點管理員 」 (EPM) 或 XLANG 尚未處理的訊息的數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-539">The “In-process messages per CPU” setting in the Host Throttling Settings is the maximum number of messages delivered to the End Point Manager (EPM) or XLANG that have not been processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-540">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk 訊息代理程式內含式訊息計數節流閾值分析本主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-540">For more information, refer to BizTalk Message Agent In-process Message Count Throttling Threshold Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-541">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 訊息代理程式處理序記憶體使用量 (MB) 節流設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-541">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Message Agent Process Memory Usage (MB) Throttling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-542">這是目前的處理序 (MB) 的記憶體使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-542">This is the memory usage of current process (MB).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-543">BizTalk 處理序記憶體節流設定可能要發行批次具有並不容易學習的記憶體需求，或是太多的執行緒正在處理訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-543">BizTalk process memory throttling can occur if the batch to be published has steep memory requirements, or if too many threads are processing messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-544">如需詳細資訊，請參閱本主題中的 BizTalk 訊息代理程式處理序記憶體使用量 (MB) 節流分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-544">For more information, refer to BizTalk Message Agent Process Memory Usage (MB) Throttling Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-545">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 訊息代理程式處理序記憶體使用量 (MB) 節流處理臨界值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-545">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Message Agent Process Memory Usage (MB) Throttling Threshold</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-546">這是目前的處理序 (MB) 的記憶體使用量的目前閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-546">This is the current threshold for the memory usage of current process (MB).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-547">實際至這個處理序記憶體耗用量模式，其可用的記憶體數量而定，可能會以動態方式調整臨界值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-547">The threshold may be dynamically adjusted depending on the actual amount of memory available to this process and its memory consumption pattern.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-548">BizTalk 處理序記憶體節流設定可能要發行批次具有並不容易學習的記憶體需求，或是太多的執行緒正在處理訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-548">BizTalk process memory throttling can occur if the batch to be published has steep memory requirements, or if too many threads are processing messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-549">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 BizTalk 訊息代理程式處理序記憶體使用量 (MB) 本主題中的節流閾值分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-549">For more information, refer to BizTalk Message Agent Process memory usage (MB) Throttling Threshold Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-550">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 訊息代理程式執行緒計數節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-550">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Message Agent Thread Count Throttling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-551">BizTalk 處理序中執行緒的總數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-551">The total number of threads in the BizTalk process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-552">[每一 CPU 的執行緒] 是在主機處理程序包括使用配接器之執行緒的執行緒總數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-552">“Threads Per CPU” is the total number of threads in the host process including threads used by adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-553">若超過此閾值，BizTalk Server 會嘗試減少 EPM 執行緒集區和訊息代理程式執行緒集區的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-553">If this threshold is exceeded, BizTalk Server will try to reduce the size of EPM thread pool and message agent thread pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-554">在高負載可能導致建立大量執行緒的情況時，應啟用以執行緒為基礎的節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-554">Thread based throttling should be enabled in scenarios where high load can lead to the creation of a large number of threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-555">此參數會同時影響輸入和輸出節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-555">This parameter affects both inbound and outbound throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-556">執行緒為基礎的節流預設為停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-556">Thread based throttling is disabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-557">這項分析會檢查 BizTalk 執行緒計數是否大於 80%的指出節流狀況有可能節流臨界值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-557">This analysis checks whether the BizTalk Thread count is greater than 80 percent of the throttling threshold value indicating a throttling condition is likely.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-558">參考：</span><span |<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-564">BizTalk Server: BizTalk 訊息代理程式執行緒計數節流處理臨界值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-564">BizTalk Server:  BizTalk Message Agent Thread Count Throttling the process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-566">[每一 CPU 的執行緒] 是在主機處理程序包括使用配接器之執行緒的執行緒總數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-566">“Threads Per CPU” is the total number of whether this throttling setting is set to a non-default value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-571">執行緒為基礎的節流預設為停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-571">Thread based Throttling Performance Counters at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155285](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155285)</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-574">-如何[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]實作主控件節流在 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155286](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155286)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-574">-   How [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] Implements Host Throttling at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155286](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155286)</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-575">-如何修改預設主控件節流設定 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155296](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155296)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-575">-   How to Modify the Default Host Throttling Settings at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155296](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155296)</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-576">-影響配接器的效能設定參數 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=154200](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=154200)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-576">-   Configuration Parameters that Affect Adapter Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=154200](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=154200)</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-577">執行緒，資料庫工作階段，並在節流 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-577">-   Threads, DB sessions, and throttling at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793)</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="logicalphysical-disk-readwrite-latency-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-578">邏輯/實體磁碟讀取/寫入延遲分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-578">Logical/Physical Disk Read/Write Latency Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-579">Windows 偵測到磁碟的效能瓶頸最可靠的方式是藉由測量其回應時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-579">The most reliable way for Windows to detect a disk performance bottleneck is by measuring its response times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-580">如果回應時間大於.025 （25 毫秒為單位），也就是保守的臨界值，然後值得注意的速度並影響使用者的效能問題可能會發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-580">If the response times are greater than .025 (25 milliseconds), which is a conservative threshold, then noticeable slow-downs and performance issues affecting users may be occurring.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-581">不佳的磁碟延遲的常見原因是磁碟分散程度，能快取、 使用量飽和 SAN，並在磁碟上的負載過大。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-581">Common causes of poor disk latency are disk fragmentation, performance cache, an over saturated SAN, and too much load on the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-582">使用 SPA 工具，找出的最上層檔案和使用磁碟的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-582">Use the SPA tool to help identify the top files and processes using the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-583">同時檢查 」 程序 IO Data Operations/sec"和"處理序 IO 其他 Operations/sec"，了解哪些處理程序會使用最大磁碟我 / O 的</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-583">Also check the “Process IO Data Operations/sec” and “Process IO Other Operations/sec” to see which processes are consuming the most disk I/O’s.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-584">請注意，效能監視器計數器無法指定哪些檔案相關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-584">Keep in mind that performance monitor counters are unable to specify which files are involved.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="references"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-585">參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-585">References</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-587">如何識別使用 Microsoft 伺服器效能警告器 (SPA) 工具，在磁碟效能瓶頸 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98096](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98096)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-587">How to Identify a Disk Performance Bottleneck Using the Microsoft Server Performance Advisor (SPA) Tool at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98096](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98096)</span></span>

## <a name="logical-disk-transferssec"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-589">Logical Disk Transfers/sec</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-589">Logical Disk Transfers/sec</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-590">「 磁碟 Transfers/sec"是讀取的速率和寫入磁碟上的作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-590">“Disk Transfers/sec” is the rate of read and write operations on the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-591">由於磁碟轉移操作並不直接的相互關聯的磁碟我 / O 的它們告訴我們多少磁碟作業正在進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-591">While disk transfers are not a direct correlation to disk I/O's, they do tell us how many disk operations are occurring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-592">如果您平均循序我 / O 的隨機和我 / O 的則您最後產生約 80 我 / O 的每秒做為一般的經驗法則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-592">If you average out sequential I/O’s and random I/O's, then you end up with about 80 I/O's per second as a general rule of thumb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-593">因此，我們應該預期 SAN 磁碟機執行我超過 80/O 的每個底下的第二個 when 載入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-593">Therefore, we should expect a SAN drive to perform more than 80 I/O's per second when under load.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-594">這項分析檢查以查看是否有任何的邏輯磁碟的臨界值會顯示不佳的回應時間 （大於 25 毫秒 I/O 作業的回應時間）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-594">The thresholds for this analysis check to see whether any of the logical disks are showing poor response times (greater than 25 ms response times for I/O operations).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-595">如果為 true，我們應該預期會等於或高於 80 每秒磁碟轉移操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-595">If this is true, then we should expect the disk transfers per second to be at or above 80.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-596">如果沒有，則需要調查磁碟架構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-596">If not, then the disk architecture needs to be investigated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-597">不佳的磁碟 I/O 的最常見原因是多載 SAN – 這表示的條件的多個 LUN 使用小型的實體磁碟陣列上的邏輯單元編號 (LUN)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-597">The most common cause of poor disk I/O is logical unit number (LUN) overloading on the SAN – meaning the condition where more than one LUN is using the small physical disk array.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-598">참조</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-598">Reference</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-599">NT 伺服器和磁碟子系統效能 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-599">NT Server and Disk Subsystem Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="available-memory-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-600">可用記憶體分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-600">Available Memory Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-601">"Available Mbytes 」 是以 mb 為單位的電腦上執行的處理序可用的實體記憶體數量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-601">“Available Mbytes” is the amount of physical memory available to processes running on the computer, in megabytes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-602">虛擬記憶體管理員持續調整用於維護最小作業系統和處理序的可用位元組數目的實體記憶體中和磁碟上的空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-602">The Virtual Memory Manager continually adjusts the space used in physical memory and on disk to maintain a minimum number of available bytes for the operating system and processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-603">當可用的位元組是充足，虛擬記憶體管理員可讓處理程序的工作集成長時，或將它們置於穩定藉由移除舊的頁面加入每一個新頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-603">When available bytes are plentiful, the Virtual Memory Manager lets the working sets of processes grow, or keeps them stable by removing an old page for each new page added.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-604">可用的位元組數時，虛擬記憶體管理員必須修剪處理程序來維護所需的最小工作的集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-604">When available bytes are few, the Virtual Memory Manager must trim the working sets of processes to maintain the minimum required.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-605">這項分析會檢查，看看是否低 – 警告位於可用的 10%的總可用記憶體和 5%的可用的重大。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-605">This analysis checks to see whether the total available memory is low – Warning at 10 percent available and Critical at 5 percent available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-606">遞減趨勢 10 MB 的每小時偵測到，指出潛在的即將進行的記憶體不足時，也會提出警示警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-606">A warning is also alerted when a decreasing trend of 10 MB’s per hour is detected, indicating a potential upcoming memory condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-607">實體記憶體不足可能會造成更高特殊權限的模式 CPU 和系統的延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-607">Low physical memory can cause increased privileged mode CPU and system delays.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="references"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-608">參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-608">References</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-610">統治出記憶體繫結的問題 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-610">Ruling Out Memory-Bound Problems at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="memory-leak-detection-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-611">記憶體流失偵測分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-611">Memory Leak Detection Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-612">這項分析會判斷是否的任何程序正在耗用大量系統的記憶體和處理程序是否在經過一段時間的記憶體耗用量增加。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-612">This analysis determines whether any of the processes are consuming a large amount of the system's memory and whether the process is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-613">處理序耗用的記憶體也沒關係，只要在處理序傳回回系統的記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-613">A process consuming large portions of memory is okay as long as the process returns the memory back to the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-614">尋找增加圖表中的趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-614">Look for increasing trends in the chart.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-615">遞增趨勢上很長一段時間可能表示記憶體流失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-615">An increasing trend over a long period of time could indicate a memory leak.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-616">私用位元組是目前的大小，以位元組為單位，此處理序已配置的記憶體不能與其他處理序共用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-616">Private Bytes is the current size, in bytes, of memory that this process has allocated that cannot be shared with other processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-617">這項分析會檢查 10 MB 的每小時和 5 MB 的每小時增加的趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-617">This analysis checks for 10 MB’s per hour and 5 MB’s per hour increasing trends.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-618">您可以使用這項分析中可用的記憶體分析相互關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-618">Use this analysis in correlation with the Available Memory analysis.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-619">此外，請記住，啟動新的程序一開始會顯示為記憶體流失時，它只是正常的啟動行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-619">Also, keep in mind that newly started processes will initially appear as a memory leak when it is simply normal startup behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-620">處理序耗用的記憶體會繼續與一段很長一段時間不釋放記憶體時發生記憶體流失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-620">A memory leak occurs when a process continues to consume memory and does not release memory over a long period of time.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-621">如果您懷疑記憶體流失的狀況，再安裝，並使用偵錯診斷工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-621">If you suspect a memory leak condition, then install and use the Debug Diag tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-622">如需有關偵錯診斷工具的詳細資訊，請參閱 < 參考一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-622">For more information on the Debug Diag Tool, see the references section.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-623">참조</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-623">Reference</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-624">偵錯診斷工具 v1.1，在 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-624">Debug Diagnostic Tool v1.1 at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="memory-pagessec-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-625">記憶體每秒頁面分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-625">Memory Pages/sec Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-626">這項分析會檢查，看看是否高"Pages/sec"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-626">This analysis checks to see whether the “Pages/sec” is high.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-627">如果高，然後系統可能記憶體不足嘗試將頁面上的記憶體到磁碟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-627">If it is high, then the system is likely running out of memory by trying to page the memory to the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-628">「 頁/sec"是在讀取或寫入為解決硬體分頁錯誤而對磁碟頁面的速率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-628">“Pages/sec” is the rate at which pages are read from or written to disk to resolve hard page faults.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-629">這個計數器是導致整個系統延遲的錯誤種類的主要指示器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-629">This counter is a primary indicator of the kinds of faults that cause system-wide delays.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-630">它是 「 Memory\Pages Input/sec"和"Memory\Pages Output/sec"的總和。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-630">It is the sum of “Memory\Pages Input/sec” and “Memory\Pages Output/sec”.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-631">它被計算頁數，因此可以與其他分頁數，例如"Memory\Page Faults/sec"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-631">It is counted in numbers of pages, so it can be compared to other counts of pages, such as “Memory\Page Faults/sec”.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-632">此計數器一律應少於 1000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-632">This counter should always be below 1,000.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-633">這項分析會檢查超過 1,000 個的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-633">This analysis checks for values above 1,000.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-634">使用這項分析中可用的記憶體分析和記憶體流失偵測分析與相互關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-634">Use this analysis in correlation with Available Memory Analysis and Memory Leak Detection analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-635">如果所有的分析在同一時間中擲回警示，這可能表示系統用完記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-635">If all analyses are throwing alerts at the same time, then this may indicate the system is running out of memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-636">請遵循本主題中的其他資訊有關記憶體流失偵測分析中所述的分析步驟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-636">Follow analysis steps mentioned in Additional Information Regarding Memory Leak Detection analysis in this topic.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-637">참조</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-637">Reference</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-638">統治出記憶體繫結的問題 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-638">Ruling Out Memory-Bound Problems at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="memory-system-cache-resident-bytes-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-639">記憶體系統快取常駐位元組分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-639">Memory System Cache Resident Bytes Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-640">「 系統快取常駐位元組 」 是大小，以位元組為單位的檔案系統快取中的可分頁作業系統程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-640">“System Cache Resident Bytes” is the size, in bytes, of the pageable operating system code in the file system cache.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-641">此值只包含目前實體頁面，而且不包含任何非目前駐留的虛擬記憶體分頁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-641">This value includes only current physical pages and does not include any virtual memory pages not currently resident.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-642">它等於顯示 [工作管理員] 中的系統快取值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-642">It does equal the System Cache value shown in Task Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-643">如此一來，這個值可能小於的實際使用中的檔案系統快取的虛擬記憶體數量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-643">As a result, this value may be smaller than the actual amount of virtual memory in use by the file system cache.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-644">這個值是元件的 「 記憶體\\\System 常駐位元組的程式碼 」，代表所有目前正在實體記憶體的可分頁作業系統程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-644">This value is a component of “Memory\\\System Code Resident Bytes”, which represents all pageable operating system code that is currently in physical memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-645">這個計數器會顯示最後觀察到的值它不是平均值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-645">This counter displays the last observed value only; it is not an average.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-646">這項分析會檢查每小時 10 MB 的遞增趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-646">This analysis checks for an increasing trend of 10 MB’s per hour.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-647">在負載下，伺服器可能會以快取的 I/O 活動，例如磁碟使用的系統快取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-647">Under load, a server might use the system cache in order to cache I/O activity such as disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-648">用於相互關聯處理序 IO Data Operations/sec 與其他處理序 IO 作業數/秒的分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-648">Use in correlation with Process IO Data Operations/sec and Process IO Other Operations/sec analyses.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="processor-utilization-analysis-and-excessive-processor-use-by-processes"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-649">處理器使用率分析和處理序過度佔用處理器使用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-649">Processor Utilization Analysis and Excessive Processor Use by Processes</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-650">「 處理器時間百分比 」 是處理器花費在執行非閒置執行緒所經過時間的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-650">“% Processor Time” is the percentage of elapsed time that the processor spends to execute a non-idle thread.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-651">其計算方式是測量閒置執行緒處於使用中的範例間隔的持續時間，然後再從減去該時間間隔的持續時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-651">It is calculated by measuring the duration the idle thread is active in the sample interval, and then subtracting that time from the interval duration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-652">（每顆處理器具有閒置執行緒會佔用循環當其他執行緒尚未準備好要執行的）。此計數器是處理器活動的主要指示器，並顯示在取樣間隔期間觀察到的忙碌時間平均百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-652">(Each processor has an idle thread that consumes cycles when no other threads are ready to run.) This counter is the primary indicator of processor activity and displays the average percentage of busy time observed during the sample interval.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-653">其計算方式是監視該服務處於非使用中的時間，並從 100%減去該值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-653">It is calculated by monitoring the time that the service is inactive, and subtracting that value from 100 percent.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-654">這項分析會檢查使用量大於每個個別的處理器上的 60%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-654">This analysis checks for utilization greater than 60 percent on each individual processor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-655">如果是的話，判斷它是否高使用者模式 CPU 或高特殊權限的模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-655">If so, determine whether it is high user mode CPU or high privileged mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-656">如果懷疑 CPU 高特殊權限的模式，則會看到 「 特殊權限模式 CPU 分析 」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-656">If high privileged mode CPU is suspected, then see the “Privileged Mode CPU Analysis”.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-657">如果懷疑有使用者模式處理器瓶頸，請考慮使用處理程序的程式碼剖析工具分析造成高 CPU 耗用率的函式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-657">If a user-mode processor bottleneck is suspected, then consider using a process profiler to analyze the functions causing the high CPU consumption.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-658">請參閱 「 如何以： 識別造成高的使用者模式 CPU 瓶頸的伺服器應用程式在生產環境中的函式 」 參考一節，如需詳細資訊的發行項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-658">See “How To: Identify Functions causing a High User-mode CPU Bottleneck for Server Applications in a Production Environment” article in the references section for more information.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="processor-queue-length-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-659">處理器佇列長度分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-659">Processor Queue Length Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-660">「 處理器佇列長度 」 是處理器佇列中的執行緒數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-660">“Processor Queue Length” is the number of threads in the processor queue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-661">不同於磁碟計數器，此計數器會顯示準備就緒的執行緒，無法執行的執行緒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-661">Unlike the disk counters, this counter shows ready threads only, not threads that are running.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-662">即使在有多個處理器的電腦上，有處理器時間是單一佇列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-662">There is a single queue for processor time even on computers with multiple processors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-663">因此，如果電腦有多個處理器，您需要此值除以工作負載的處理器數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-663">Therefore, if a computer has multiple processors, you need to divide this value by the number of processors servicing the workload.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-664">處理器佇列持續少於 10 個執行緒，每個處理器的是可以接受的依存工作負載。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-664">A sustained processor queue of less than 10 threads per processor is normally acceptable, dependent of the workload.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-665">這項分析會判斷是否平均處理器佇列長度會超過處理器的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-665">This analysis determines whether the average processor queue length exceeds the number of processors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-666">如果是的話，這可能表示發生處理器瓶頸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-666">If so, then this could indicate a processor bottleneck.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-667">使用這項分析中使用特殊權限模式 CPU 分析和處理程序過多處理器使用相互關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-667">Use this analysis in correlation with Privileged Mode CPU Analysis and Excessive Processor Use by Process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-668">處理器佇列已準備好，但您不能因為另一個使用中執行緒目前正在執行的處理器來執行執行緒的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-668">The processor queue is the collection of threads that are ready but not able to be executed by the processor because another active thread is currently executing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-669">持續性或重複執行的多個執行緒的處理器數目超過佇列可清楚指出是處理器瓶頸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-669">A sustained or recurring queue of more threads than number of processors is a good indication of a processor bottleneck.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-670">您可以使用這個計數器配合"處理器\\%Processor Time"計數器以判斷您的應用程式是否可以發揮更多的 Cpu。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-670">You can use this counter in conjunction with the “Processor\\% Processor Time” counter to determine whether your application can benefit from more CPUs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-671">沒有單一佇列的處理器時間，即使在多處理器電腦上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-671">There is a single queue for processor time, even on multiprocessor computers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-672">因此，在多處理器電腦上，「 處理器佇列長度 」 (PQL) 值除以工作負載的處理器數目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-672">Therefore, in a multiprocessor computer, divide the “Processor Queue Length” (PQL) value by the number of processors servicing the workload</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-673">如果 CPU 是非常忙碌 （90%和更高的使用率），而且 PQL 平均值高於一致處理器數目，則您可能無法受益於額外的 Cpu 處理器瓶頸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-673">If the CPU is very busy (90 percent and higher utilization) and the PQL average is consistently higher than the number of processors, then you may have a processor bottleneck that could benefit from additional CPUs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-674">或者，您無法減少的執行緒和應用程式層級的佇列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-674">Or, you could reduce the number of threads and queue at the application level.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-675">這會導致較少的內容切換，這是適合用來降低 CPU 負載。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-675">This will cause less context switching, which is good for reducing CPU load.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-676">處理器時間的要求到達隨機，而執行緒要求異常大量的處理器時間高 PQL 低 CPU 使用率的常見原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-676">The common reason for a high PQL with low CPU utilization is that requests for processor time arrive randomly, and threads demand irregular amounts of time from the processor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-677">這表示處理器不是瓶頸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-677">This means that the processor is not a bottleneck.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-678">相反地，將執行緒的邏輯，需要改善。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-678">Instead, your threading logic that needs to be improved.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-679">如果懷疑有使用者模式處理器瓶頸，請考慮使用處理程序的程式碼剖析工具分析造成高 CPU 耗用率的函式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-679">If a user-mode processor bottleneck is suspected, then consider using a process profiler to analyze the functions causing the high CPU consumption.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-680">請參閱 「 如何以： 識別造成高的使用者模式 CPU 瓶頸的伺服器應用程式在生產環境中的函式 」 參考一節，如需詳細資訊的發行項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-680">See the “How To: Identify Functions causing a High User-mode CPU Bottleneck for Server Applications in a Production Environment” article in the references section for more information.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="privileged-mode-cpu-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-681">特殊權限的模式 CPU 分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-681">Privileged Mode CPU Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-682">此計數器表示執行緒在特權模式下執行的時間的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-682">This counter indicates the percentage of time a thread runs in privileged mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-683">當您的應用程式呼叫作業系統函式 （例如來執行檔案或網路 I/O，或配置記憶體） 時，這些作業系統函式會執行特殊權限模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-683">When your application calls operating system functions (for example to perform file or network I/O or to allocate memory), these operating system functions are executed in privileged mode.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-684">高特殊權限的模式 CPU 指出電腦花太多時間在系統 I/O 與真實 （使用者模式） 的工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-684">High privileged mode CPU indicates that the computer is spending too much time in system I/O versus real (user mode) work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-685">"%特殊權限時間 」 的處理序執行緒花在特權模式下執行的程式碼的時間百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-685">“% Privileged Time” is the percentage of elapsed time that the process threads spent executing code in privileged mode.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-686">呼叫 Windows 系統服務時，服務通常會在特殊權限模式來取得系統私用資料的存取權執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-686">When a Windows system service is called, the service will often run in privileged mode to gain access to system-private data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-687">這類資料會受到在使用者模式中執行的執行緒存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-687">Such data is protected from access by threads executing in user mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-688">呼叫系統可以是明確或隱含方式，例如分頁錯誤或中斷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-688">Calls to the system can be explicit or implicit, such as page faults or interrupts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-689">與某些早期作業系統不同 Windows 會使用處理序界限來保護子系統的傳統保護除了使用者和特殊權限的模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-689">Unlike some early operating systems, Windows uses process boundaries for subsystem protection in addition to the traditional protection of user and privileged modes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-690">代表應用程式由 Windows 完成某些工作可能會出現在其他子系統處理序，除了處理序中的特殊權限時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-690">Some work done by Windows on behalf of the application might appear in other subsystem processes in addition to the privileged time in the process.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-691">這項分析會檢查是否有權限的模式 CPU 耗用超過 30%的總 CPU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-691">This analysis checks to see whether privileged mode CPU is consuming more than 30 percent of total CPU.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-692">如果，則 CPU 耗用量可能是另一個以外的處理器，例如網路、 記憶體或磁碟 I/O 瓶頸所造成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-692">If so, then the CPU consumption is likely caused by another bottleneck other than the processor such as network, memory, or disk I/O.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-693">用於相互關聯與 %Interrupt Time 及高內容切換的分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-693">Use in correlation with % Interrupt Time and High Context Switching analyses.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="high-context-switching-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-694">高內容切換分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-694">High Context Switching Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-695">當高優先順序的執行緒優先執行較低優先順序的執行緒目前正在執行或高優先權執行緒會封鎖，就會發生內容切換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-695">A context switch happens when a higher priority thread preempts a lower priority thread that is currently running or when a high priority thread blocks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-696">多執行緒共用相同的優先權層級，就會發生內容切換的高層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-696">High levels of context switching can occur when many threads share the same priority level.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-697">這通常表示太多執行緒會在系統上處理器的競爭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-697">This often indicates that too many threads are competing for the processors on the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-698">如果您看不太多的處理器使用率，而且您看到的內容切換的層級非常低，則可能表示執行緒會被封鎖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-698">If you do not see much processor utilization and you see very low levels of context switching, it could indicate that threads are blocked.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-699">高內容切換只應該加以調查，高 CPU 和整體 CPU 的特殊權限的模式時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-699">High context switching should only be investigated when privileged mode CPU and overall CPU is high.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-700">一般而言，內容切換率小於每個處理器每秒 5000 就不值得耽心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-700">As a general rule, context switching rates of less than 5,000 per second per processor are not worth worrying about.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-701">如果內容切換率超過 15,000 每個處理器每秒，就將條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-701">If context switching rates exceed 15,000 per second per processor, then there is a constraint.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-702">這項分析會檢查是否有高的 CPU、 高特殊權限的模式 CPU 和高 （超過 5000，每個處理器） 系統秒內容切換次數所有發生在相同的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-702">This analysis checks for high CPU, high privileged mode CPU, and high (greater than 5,000 per processor) system context switches per second all occurring at the same time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-703">如果發生高內容切換時，接著減少執行緒和處理序在系統上執行的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-703">If high context switching is occurring, then reduce the number of threads and processes running on the system.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="biztalk-high-database-sessions-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-704">BizTalk 高資料庫工作階段分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-704">BizTalk High Database Sessions Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-705">此計數器會有兩個可能的值也就是正常 (0)，或超過 (1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-705">This counter has two possible values namely normal (0) or exceeded (1).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-706">這項分析會檢查值為 1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-706">This analysis checks for a value of 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-707">如果是這樣，BizTalk 已超過允許的資料庫工作階段數目的臨界值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-707">If so, BizTalk has exceeded the threshold of the number of database sessions permitted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-708">這個值是由 「 每一 CPU 的資料庫連線 」 中的值的 BizTalk 主控件節流設定所控制的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-708">This value is controlled by the “Database connection per CPU” value in the BizTalk Host Throttling settings.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-709">「 資料庫每一 CPU 的連線 」 為並行資料庫工作階段數目上限 （每一 CPU) 節流開始前允許。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-709">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-710">一般個別主控件工作階段集區中的閒置資料庫工作階段不會加到此計數，而是對主控件執行個體實際正在使用的工作階段數目嚴格執行這項檢查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-710">The idle database sessions in the common per-host session pool do not add to this count, and this check is made strictly on the number of sessions actually being used by the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-711">此選項會停用的預設值;一般而言，這項設定，才應該啟用如果資料庫伺服器是瓶頸或低階的資料庫伺服器的 BizTalk Server 系統中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-711">This option is disabled by default; typically, this setting should only be enabled if the database server is a bottleneck or for low-end database servers in the BizTalk Server system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-712">您可以使用 biztalk： 訊息代理程式的效能物件類別下的資料庫工作階段效能計數器監視使用中的資料庫連線數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-712">You can monitor the number of active database connections by using the database session performance counter under the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-713">此參數只會影響輸出訊息節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-713">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-714">輸入值為 0 時可停用以資料庫工作階段數目為基礎的節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-714">Enter a value of 0 to disable throttling that is based on the number of database sessions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-715">預設值是 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-715">The default value is 0.</span></span>  
  
> [!NOTE]  
>  <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-716">「 MaxWorkerThreads"登錄機碼會影響數字的執行緒可用來 BizTalk 和有助於如果大部分的 BizTalk 執行緒忙著處理資料庫連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-716">The “MaxWorkerThreads” registry key influences the number threads available to BizTalk and may help if most of the BizTalk threads are busy with database connections.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-high-database-size-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-722">BizTalk 高資料庫大小分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-722">BizTalk High Database Size Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-723">此計數器是指在此程序已發佈的資料庫佇列中的訊息數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-723">This counter refers to the number of messages in the database queues that this process has published.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-724">這個值是由所有主控件的佇列表格中之項目數目以及多工緩衝處理與追蹤表格中的項目數目來測量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-724">This value is measured by the number of items in the queue tables for all hosts and the number of items in the spool and tracking tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-725">佇列包含在工作佇列、 狀態佇列和擱置的佇列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-725">Queue includes the work queue, the state queue and the suspended queue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-726">若程序正發佈到多個佇列，則此計數器會反映所有佇列的加權平均值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-726">If a process is publishing to multiple queues, this counter reflects the weighted average of all the queues.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-727">若重新啟動主控件，則會遺失保留在記憶體中的統計值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-727">If the host is restarted, statistics held in memory are lost.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-728">涉及一些額外負荷，因為 BizTalk Server 將會繼續收集統計資料，只有當有至少 100 發行時，具有 5%的總計會發佈在重新啟動主控件程序中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-728">Since some overhead is involved, BizTalk Server will resume gathering statistics only when there are at least 100 publishes, with 5 percent of the total publishes within the restarted host process.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-729">此計數器將設定為值 1，如果其中一個列出的資料庫臨界值中的訊息計數的條件發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-729">This counter will be set to a value of 1 if either of the conditions listed for the message count in database threshold occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-730">此閾值記錄主題中的 < 如何修改預設主控件節流設定下面所參照。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-730">This threshold is documented in the topic How to Modify the Default Host Throttling Settings referenced below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-731">根據預設主機訊息資料庫節流閾值中的計數是設定為 50000，將會觸發節流狀況，在下列情況下的值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-731">By default the host message count in database throttling threshold is set to a value of 50,000, which will trigger a throttling condition under the following circumstances:</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-732">主控件執行個體發佈到訂閱之主控件的工作、狀態和擱置佇列的訊息總數超過 50,000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-732">The total number of messages published by the host instance to the work, state, and suspended queues of the subscribing hosts exceeds 50,000.</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-733">多工緩衝處理表格或追蹤表格中的訊息數目超過 50,000 個訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-733">The number of messages in the spool table or the tracking table exceeds 500,000 messages.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-734">即使低或完全無負載發生 BizTalk server 擱置的訊息包含在計算資料庫中的訊息計數，因為是的訊息發佈節流可能發生的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-734">Since suspended messages are included in the message count in database calculation, throttling of message publishing can occur even if the BizTalk server is experiencing low or no load.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-735">這項分析會檢查值為 1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-735">This analysis checks for a value of 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-736">如果發生這種情況，請考慮採取的動作，將會減少在資料庫中的訊息數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-736">If this occurs, then consider a course of action that will reduce the number of messages in the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-737">比方說，確保 BizTalk SQL Server 正在執行工作不會發生錯誤，並在 BizTalk 管理主控台中使用 群組中樞，以判斷是否要將訊息增多造成的大量擱置的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-737">For example, ensure the BizTalk SQL Server jobs are running without error and use the Group Hub in the BizTalk Administration console to determine whether message build up is caused by large numbers of suspended messages.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-739">擱置的訊息會包含在資料庫節流閾值中郵件計數 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155304](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155304)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-739">Suspended Messages are Included in the Message Count in Database Throttling Threshold at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155304](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155304)</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-high-in-process-message-count-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-742">BizTalk 高內含式訊息計數分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-742">BizTalk High In-Process Message Count Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-743">「 內含式訊息每一 CPU 」 中的設定主控件節流設定是傳遞至 「 結束點管理員 」 (EPM) 或 XLANG 尚未處理的訊息的數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-743">The “In-process messages per CPU” setting in the Host Throttling Settings is the maximum number of messages delivered to the End Point Manager (EPM) or XLANG that have not been processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-744">這個數字不包含擷取自資料庫，但仍然等候中記憶體中的佇列傳遞的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-744">This number does not include the messages retrieved from database but still waiting for delivery in the in-memory queue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-745">您可以使用 biztalk： 訊息代理程式的效能物件類別下的 內含式訊息計數 效能計數器來監視內含式訊息的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-745">You can monitor the number of in-Process Messages by using the In-process message count performance counter under the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-746">當您考慮節流狀況時，這個參數會提供提示給節流機制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-746">This parameter provides a hint to the throttling mechanism when considering throttling conditions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-747">實際閾值會受自我調整影響而不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-747">The actual threshold is subject to self-tuning.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-748">您可以監視內含式訊息計數 」 效能計數器，以確認實際閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-748">You can verify the actual threshold by monitoring the in-process message count performance counter.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-749">這個參數可以將大型訊息實例，其中平均訊息大小很高，或訊息的處理可能需要大量的訊息較小的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-749">This parameter can be set to a smaller value for large message scenarios, where either the average message size is high, or the processing of messages may require a large number of messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-750">如果案例中遇到記憶體為根據的節流太過頻繁，與記憶體臨界值可讓您取得自動調整為相當低的值，這會是明顯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-750">This would be evident if a scenario experiences memory-based throttling too often and if the memory threshold gets auto-adjusted to a substantially low value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-751">此類行為發生時表示輸出傳輸應減少同時處理的訊息數，以避免過度使用記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-751">Such behavior would indicate that the outbound transport should process fewer messages concurrently to avoid excessive memory usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-752">此外，對於一次處理少量訊息可讓配接器較有效率的實例 (例如，傳送至限制並行連線的伺服器時)，此參數可調整為低於預設的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-752">Also, for scenarios where the adapter is more efficient when processing a few messages at a time (for example, when sending to a server that limits concurrent connections), this parameter may be tuned to a lower value than the default.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-753">這項分析會檢查以判斷是否發生這種節流高內含式訊息計數計數器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-753">This analysis checks the High In-Process Message Count counter to determine whether this kind of throttling is occurring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-754">如果是的話，請考慮調整"訊息每一 CPU 的內含式 」 設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-754">If so, consider adjusting the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-755">此參數只會影響輸出訊息節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-755">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-756">在停用以每一 CPU 的內含式訊息數目為基礎的節流"訊息每一 CPU 的內含式 」 設定中輸入值為 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-756">Enter a value of 0 in the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting to disable throttling based on the number of in-process messages per CPU.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-757">「 內含式訊息每一 CPU 」 設定的預設值是 1000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-757">The default value for the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting is 1,000.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-758">請注意，此值也可能會影響低度延遲的訊息和 （或） BizTalk 資源的效率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-758">Note that modifying this value can also have an impact on low latency of messages and/or the efficiency of BizTalk resources.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-761">主控件節流效能計數器在 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155285](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155285)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-761">Host Throttling Performance Counters at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155285](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155285)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="biztalk-high-message-delivery-rate-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-762">BizTalk 高訊息傳遞速率分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-762">BizTalk High Message Delivery Rate Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-763">對於輸出 （已傳遞） 訊息，BizTalk Server 會調整訊息的傳遞如果主控件執行個體的訊息傳遞內送速率超過訊息傳遞外寄速率 \* 指定的速率增加因數 （百分比） 值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-763">For outbound (delivered) messages, BizTalk Server throttles delivery of messages if the message delivery incoming rate for the host instance exceeds the message delivery outgoing rate \* the specified rate overdrive factor (percent) value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-764">訊息處理節流設定 對話方塊上的速率增加因數 （百分比） 參數是可設定的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-764">The rate overdrive factor (percent) parameter is configurable on the Message Processing Throttling Settings dialog box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-765">主要是藉由引發從記憶體中佇列移除訊息，並將訊息傳遞到結束點管理員 」 (EPM) 或協調流程引擎以進行處理之前的延遲來完成輸出訊息之根據速率的節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-765">Rate-based throttling for outbound messages is accomplished primarily by inducing a delay before removing the messages from the in-memory queue and delivering the messages to the End Point Manager (EPM) or orchestration engine for processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-766">不採取其他任何動作的目的就能完成輸出訊息之根據速率的節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-766">No other action is taken to accomplish rate-based throttling for outbound messages.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-767">輸出節流會造成訊息延遲傳遞，而且訊息可能建立在記憶體中佇列內，並造成清除佇列執行緒遭到封鎖，直到移轉了節流狀況為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-767">Outbound throttling can cause delayed message delivery and messages may build up in the in-memory queue and cause de-queue threads to be blocked until the throttling condition is mitigated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-768">當清除佇列執行緒處於封鎖狀態、 任何其他的訊息會從 MessageBox 提取到記憶體中佇列中等待傳送外寄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-768">When de-queue threads are blocked, no additional messages are pulled from the MessageBox into the in-memory queue for outbound delivery.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-769">這項分析會檢查 1 高訊息傳遞速率計數器中的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-769">This analysis checks for a value of 1 in the High Message Delivery Rate counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-770">高訊息傳遞速率可能因高處理複雜性、 慢速輸出配接器或瞬間的系統資源不足。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-770">High message delivery rates can be caused by high processing complexity, slow outbound adapters, or a momentary shortage of system resources.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-773">BizTalk Server 如何實作主控件節流在 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155286](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155286)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-773">How BizTalk Server Implements Host Throttling at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155286](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155286)</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-high-process-memory-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-775">BizTalk 高程序記憶體分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-775">BizTalk High Process Memory Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-776">節流臨界值 設定的 BizTalk 處理序記憶體使用量會是記憶體的與工作集大小和處理序的總可用虛擬記憶體的總和，如果輸入從 1 到 100 的值使用百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-776">The BizTalk Process Memory usage throttling threshold setting is the percentage of memory used compared to the sum of the working set size and total available virtual memory for the process if a value from 1 through 100 is entered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-777">根據預設，節流設定的 BizTalk 程序記憶體使用量會是 25。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-777">By default, the BizTalk Process Memory Usage throttling setting is 25.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-778">當指定某個百分比值時，則會以定期間隔重新計算程序記憶體閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-778">When a percentage value is specified the process memory threshold is recalculated at regular intervals.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-779">如果使用者指定的百分比值，它將會以根據可用的記憶體為認可和目前的處理序記憶體使用量計算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-779">If the user specifies a percentage value, it is computed based on the available memory to commit and the current Process Memory usage.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-780">這項分析會檢查 1 高的處理序記憶體計數器的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-780">This analysis checks for a value of 1 in the High Process Memory counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-781">如果發生這種情況，然後再次嘗試使用偵錯 Diag 判斷記憶體增加的原因 （請參閱記憶體流失偵測分析中的參考）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-781">If this occurs, then try to determine the cause of the memory increase by using Debug Diag (see references in Memory Leak Detection analysis).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-782">請注意，為它的一般程序進行期間啟動，而這會耗用大量記憶體可能一開始會顯示為記憶體流失，但是當處理程序無法釋放不再需要藉此減少可用的我的記憶體時，就會發生真正的記憶體流失mory 經過一段時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-782">Note that is it normal for processes to consume a large portion of memory during startup and this may initially appear as a memory leak, but a true memory leak occurs when a process fails to release memory that it no longer needs, thereby reducing the amount of available memory over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-783">有關如何以一般方式分析程序記憶體遺漏，biztalk，請參閱下面的 「 如何要擷取記憶體傾印的處理程序，是流失記憶體 」 參考及/或 PAL 中的 「 記憶體流失偵測 」 分析，如需詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-783">See the “How to Capture a Memory Dump of a Process that is Leaking Memory” reference below and/or the “Memory Leak Detection” analysis in PAL for more information on how to generically analyze process memory leaks in BizTalk.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-784">如果要發行批次有遽記憶體需求，高程序記憶體節流設定可能會發生或太多的執行緒正在處理訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-784">High process memory throttling can occur if the batch to be published has steep memory requirements, or too many threads are processing messages.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-785">若系統出現過度節流，請考慮增加主控件相關聯處理序記憶體使用量閾值的值，並確認主控件執行個體不會產生 「 記憶體不足 」 錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-785">If the system appears to be over-throttling, consider increasing the value associated with the process memory usage threshold for the host and verify that the host instance does not generate an "out of memory" error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-786">如果藉由增加程序記憶體使用量閾值，會引發 「 記憶體不足 」 錯誤，請考慮縮減內部訊息佇列大小的值，內含式訊息，每個 CPU 臨界值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-786">If an "out of memory" error is raised by increasing the process memory usage threshold, then consider reducing the values for the internal message queue size and In-process messages per CPU thresholds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-787">此策略特別會與大型訊息處理實例有關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-787">This strategy is particularly relevant in large message processing scenarios.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-788">此外，這個值應設為需要大量記憶體需求，每個訊息的案例較低的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-788">In addition, this value should be set to a low value for scenarios having large memory requirement per message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-789">設定較低的值會在初期節流開始作用，並導致程序中的記憶體擴張。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-789">Setting a low value will kick in throttling early on and prevent a memory explosion within the process.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-790">如果您的 BizTalk server 定期執行虛擬記憶體不足，請考慮 BizTalk Server 64 位元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-790">If your BizTalk server regularly runs out of virtual memory, then consider BizTalk Server 64-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-791">在 64 位元伺服器上的每個處理序可以處理最多 4 TB 的虛擬記憶體與 2 GB 的 32 位元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-791">Each process on 64-bit servers can address up to 4 TB’s of virtual memory versus the 2 GB’s in 32-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-792">一般情況下，強烈建議 BizTalk 64 位元和 64 位元 SQL Server。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-792">In general, 64-bit BizTalk and 64-bit SQL Server is highly recommended.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-793">請參閱 < BizTalk Server 64 位元支援 > 參考，如需詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-793">See the “BizTalk Server 64-bit Support” reference for more information.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-797">如何擷取發生記憶體溢位在的處理程序的記憶體傾印 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155305](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155305)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-797">How to Capture a Memory Dump of a Process that is Leaking Memory at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155305](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155305)</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-high-system-memory-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-799">BizTalk 高系統記憶體分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-799">BizTalk High System Memory Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-800">BizTalk 的實體記憶體使用量節流臨界值設定為輸入則是從 1 到 100 相較於可用的實體記憶體的值如果總數量的記憶體耗用量的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-800">The BizTalk Physical Memory usage throttling threshold setting is the percentage of memory consumption compared to the total amount of available physical memory if a value from 1 through 100 is entered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-801">如果輸入大於 100 的值，此設定也可以是以 mb 為單位的可用實體記憶體總數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-801">This setting can also be the total amount of available physical memory in megabytes if a value greater than 100 is entered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-802">輸入值為 0 時可停用以實體記憶體使用量為基礎的節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-802">Enter a value of 0 to disable throttling based on physical memory usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-803">預設值是 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-803">The default value is 0.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-804">這項分析會檢查 1 高系統記憶體計數器的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-804">This analysis checks for a value of 1 in the High System Memory counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-805">因為這會測量系統記憶體總量，若非 BizTalk Server 程序正耗用過量的系統記憶體，則可能觸發節流狀況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-805">Since this measures total system memory, a throttling condition may be triggered if non-BizTalk Server processes are consuming an extensive amount of system memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-806">因此如果發生這種情況，最好的方法是找出哪些處理程序正在耗用的最實體記憶體及/或將額外的實體記憶體新增至伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-806">Therefore if this occurs, the best approach is to identify which processes are consuming the most physical memory and/or add additional physical memory to the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-807">此外，請考慮減少負載，藉由減少 EPM 執行緒集區的預設大小和 （或） 配接器批次的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-807">Also, consider reducing load by reducing the default size of the EPM thread pool, and/or the size of adapter batches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-808">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 < 在 PAL 中的記憶體流失偵測分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-808">For more information, see the Memory Leak Detection analysis in PAL.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-high-thread-count-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-813">BizTalk 高執行緒計數分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-813">BizTalk High Thread Count Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-814">[每一 CPU 的執行緒] 是在主機處理程序包括使用配接器之執行緒的執行緒總數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-814">“Threads Per CPU” is the total number of threads in the host process including threads used by adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-815">如果超過此臨界值時，BizTalk Server 會嘗試減少 EPM 執行緒集區和訊息代理程式 」 執行緒集區的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-815">If this threshold is exceeded, BizTalk Server will try to reduce the size of the EPM thread pool and message agent thread pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-816">在高負載可能導致建立大量執行緒的情況時，應啟用以執行緒為基礎的節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-816">Thread based throttling should be enabled in scenarios where high load can lead to the creation of a large number of threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-817">此參數會同時影響輸入和輸出節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-817">This parameter affects both inbound and outbound throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-818">執行緒為基礎的節流預設為停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-818">Thread based throttling is disabled by default.</span></span>  
  
> [!NOTE]  
>  <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-819">使用者指定的值做為指導方針，而且主應用程式可能會以動態方式自我調整為基礎的記憶體使用量模式和處理序執行緒需求此臨界值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-819">The user-specified value is used as a guideline, and the host may dynamically self-tune this threshold value based on the memory usage patterns and thread requirements of the process.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-820">這項分析會檢查 1 高執行緒計數計數器中的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-820">This analysis checks for a value of 1 in the High Thread Count counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-821">考慮調整不同的執行緒集區大小，以確定系統不會建立大量的執行緒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-821">Consider adjusting the different thread pool sizes to ensure that the system does not create a large number of threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-822">這項分析可與內容切換相互關聯每個第二個分析，以判斷是否作業系統已飽和，太多執行緒，但在大部分情況下高執行緒計數原因後端資料庫比在 BizTalk server 上的多個競爭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-822">This analysis can be correlated with Context Switches per Second analysis to determine whether the operating system is saturated with too many threads, but in most cases high thread counts cause more contention on the backend database than on the BizTalk server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-823">如需修改執行緒集區大小的詳細資訊請參閱 < 如何修改預設主控件節流設定在參考中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-823">For more information about modifying the thread pool sizes see How to Modify the Default Host Throttling Settings in references.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-830">BizTalk 輸入延遲 AnalysisAverage 延遲 （毫秒），傳訊引擎收到文件從配接器發佈至 messagebox 之前。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-830">BizTalk Inbound Latency AnalysisAverage latency in milliseconds from when the messaging engine receives a document from the adapter until the time it is published to the message box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-831">降低延遲很重要的 BizTalk 中，某些使用者因此追蹤時間文件花費輸入配接器中很重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-831">Reducing latency is important to some users of BizTalk, therefore tracking how much time documents spend in the inbound adapter is important.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-832">以下是顯示的方式測量延遲圖表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-832">Here is a chart showing how latency is measured.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-839">配接器接收訊息並提交到引擎，才能將訊息提供給引擎不在配接器完成的工作擷取這些效能計數器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-839">Adapter receives message and submits it to the engine, work done in adapter before message is given to engine not captured in these perf counters</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-840">引擎從配接器接收訊息、 執行接收管線、 對應、 訂閱評估，保存在資料庫中的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-840">Engine receives message from adapter, executes receive pipeline, map, subscription evaluation, persist message in DB.</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-841">協調流程或請求-回應連接埠執行，並產生回應訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-841">Orchestration or Solicit-Response port runs and generates a response message.</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-842">回應訊息在傳訊引擎從佇列中清除、 執行傳送管線、 對應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-842">Response message is dequeued in messaging engine, execute the send pipeline, map.</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-843">傳訊引擎會提供回應訊息給配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-843">Messaging engine gives response message to adapter.</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-844">配接器會通知引擎訊息作業都是。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-844">Adapter informs engine message is all done.</span></span>|

 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-854">I = 輸入的延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-854">I = Inbound Latency</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-855">RR = 要求的回應延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-855">RR = Request Response Latency</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-856">O = 輸出延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-856">O = Outbound Latency</span></span>
