 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-858">假設在低延遲的環境，這項分析會檢查是否在文件所花費的時間超過 5 秒的輸入配接器中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-858">Assuming a low latency environment, this analysis checks whether the document spent more than 5 seconds in the inbound adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-859">這可能表示之傳輸的訊息，透過此主控件執行個體的輸入配接器處理延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-859">This may indicate a processing delay in the transport of messages through inbound adapters in this host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-860">如果多個輸入配接器存在於此主控件執行個體，請考慮將它們分割到他們自己的主機，以判斷哪一個輸入的介面卡有高延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-860">If multiple inbound adapters exist in this host instance, then consider separating them into their own hosts to determine which inbound adapter has high latency.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-message-delivery-throttling-state-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-865">BizTalk 訊息傳遞節流狀態分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-865">BizTalk Message Delivery Throttling State Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-866">BizTalk 訊息傳遞節流狀態是節流的主要指標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-866">The BizTalk message delivery throttling state is one of the primary indicators of throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-867">它是旗標，指出系統是否正在進行節流訊息傳遞 （影響 XLANG 訊息處理及輸出傳輸）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-867">It is a flag indicating whether the system is throttling message delivery (affecting XLANG message processing and outbound transports).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-868">節流狀況會指示計數器的數值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-868">The throttling condition is indicated by the numeric value of the counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-869">以下是一份值和其各自的意義：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-869">Here is a list of the values and their respective meaning:</span></span>  
  
|||  
|-|-|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-870">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-870">0</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-871">未進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-871">Not throttling</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-872">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-872">1</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-873">由於不平衡的訊息傳遞速率 (輸入速率超過輸出速率) 而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-873">Throttling due to imbalanced message delivery rate (input rate exceeds output rate)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-874">3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-874">3</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-875">由於高內含式訊息計數而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-875">Throttling due to high in-process message count</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-876">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-876">4</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-877">由於處理程序記憶體壓力而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-877">Throttling due to process memory pressure</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-878">5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-878">5</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-879">由於系統記憶體壓力而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-879">Throttling due to system memory pressure</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-880">9</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-880">9</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-881">由於高執行緒計數而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-881">Throttling due to high thread count</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-882">10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-882">10</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-883">由於傳遞時使用者覆寫而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-883">Throttling due to user override on delivery</span></span>|  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-884">這項分析會檢查每個這些值，並為每個有特定的警示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-884">This analysis checks for each of these values and has a specific alert for each of them.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-messagebox-database-connection-failures-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-888">BizTalk MessageBox 資料庫連線失敗分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-888">BizTalk MessageBox Database Connection Failures Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-889">此效能計數器是資料庫連線嘗試的主控件執行個體啟動後失敗的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-889">This performance counter is the number of attempted database connections that failed since the host instance started.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-890">如果裝載 BizTalk 資料庫的 SQL Server 服務因故無法使用，資料庫叢集資源從作用中的電腦傳輸到被動電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-890">If the SQL Server service hosting the BizTalk databases becomes unavailable for any reason, the database cluster transfers resources from the active computer to the passive computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-891">在此容錯移轉程序期間，BizTalk Server 服務執行個體發生資料庫連接失敗並自動重新啟動以重新連接到資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-891">During this failover process, the BizTalk Server service instances experience database connection failures and automatically restart to reconnect to the databases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-892">正在運作的資料庫電腦 (先前為被動電腦) 會在容錯移轉期間獲得資源後，開始處理資料庫連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-892">The functioning database computer (previously the passive computer) begins processing the database connections after assuming the resources during failover.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-893">當 BizTalk Server 執行階段無法與 MessageBox 或管理資料庫通訊時，會發生 DBNetLib （資料庫網路程式庫） 錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-893">DBNetLib (Database Network Library) errors occur when the BizTalk Server runtime is unable to communicate with either the MessageBox or management databases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-894">當發生這種情況時，攔截例外狀況的 BizTalk Server 執行階段執行個體就會關閉，並再每分鐘循環查看資料庫是否可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-894">When this occurs, the BizTalk Server runtime instance that catches the exception shuts down and then cycles every minute to check to see whether the database is available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-895">這個主題，請參閱 [參考] 區段，如需詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-895">See the references section for more information on this topic.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-896">當用戶端起始 TCP/IP 通訊端連線聯繫伺服器時，用戶端通常會連接到伺服器上特定的連接埠，並要求伺服器透過短期有效的臨時 TCP 或 UDP 連接埠回應用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-896">When a client initiates a TCP/IP socket connection to a server, the client typically connects to a specific port on the server and requests that the server respond to the client over an ephemeral, or short lived, TCP or UDP port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-897">在 Windows Server 2003 和 Windows XP 中，用戶端應用程式所使用的臨時連接埠的預設範圍是從 1025 到 5000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-897">On Windows Server 2003 and Windows XP, the default range of ephemeral ports used by client applications is from 1025 through 5000.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-898">在某些情況下很可能就會耗盡可用的連接埠中的預設範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-898">Under certain conditions it is possible that the available ports in the default range will be exhausted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-899">這個主題，請參閱 [參考] 區段，如需詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-899">See the references section for more information on this topic.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-900">這項分析會檢查資料庫連線失敗的任何項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-900">This analysis checks for any occurrence of database connection failures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-901">資料庫連線失敗非常重要的因為 BizTalk 資料庫沒有就無法作用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-901">Database connection failures are critical because BizTalk cannot function without the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-902">如果資料庫連線失敗的原因不明，然後考慮下面所列的參考和/或連絡 Microsoft 支援服務以判斷連線失敗的性質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-902">If the cause of the database connection failure is unknown, then consider the references listed below and/or contact Microsoft Support to determine the nature of the connectivity failure.</span></span>

    [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155309](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155309)  
  
## <a name="biztalk-messaging-publishing-throttling-state-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-907">BizTalk 訊息發佈節流狀態分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-907">BizTalk Messaging Publishing Throttling State Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-908">BizTalk 訊息發佈節流狀態是節流的主要指標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-908">The BizTalk message publishing throttling state is one of the primary indicators of throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-909">旗標，指出系統是否正在進行節流 （影響 XLANG 訊息處理及輸入的傳輸） 的訊息發佈它。節流狀況會指示計數器的數值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-909">It is a flag indicating whether the system is throttling message publishing (affecting XLANG message processing and inbound transports).The throttling condition is indicated by the numeric value of the counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-910">以下是一份值和其各自的意義：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-910">Here is a list of the values and their respective meaning:</span></span>  
  
|||  
|-|-|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-911">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-911">0</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-912">未進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-912">Not throttling</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-913">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-913">2</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-914">由於不平衡的訊息發佈速率 (輸入速率超過輸出速率) 而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-914">Throttling due to imbalanced message publishing rate (input rate exceeds output rate)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-915">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-915">4</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-916">由於處理程序記憶體壓力而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-916">Throttling due to process memory pressure</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-917">5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-917">5</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-918">由於系統記憶體壓力而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-918">Throttling due to system memory pressure</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-919">6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-919">6</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-920">由於資料庫成長而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-920">Throttling due to database growth</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-921">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-921">8</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-922">由於高工作階段計數而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-922">Throttling due to high session count</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-923">9</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-923">9</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-924">由於高執行緒計數而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-924">Throttling due to high thread count</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-925">11</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-925">11</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9fc74-926">由於發佈時使用者覆寫而進行節流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-926">Throttling due to user override on publishing</span></span>|  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-927">這項分析會檢查每個這些值，並為每個有特定的警示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-927">This analysis checks for each of these values and has a specific alert for each of them.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="references"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-928">參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-928">References</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-orchestrations-resident-in-memory"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-931">在記憶體中的 BizTalk 協調流程內建</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-931">BizTalk Orchestrations Resident in Memory</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-932">目前由主控件執行個體裝載的協調流程執行個體數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-932">Number of orchestration instances currently hosted by the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-933">如果看到爆增情形或暴增的記憶體中駐留的協調流程可能遭視為正常，而遞增趨勢可能表示"以免 」 的協調流程在記憶體中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-933">While spikes or bursts of orchestrations resident in memory may be considered normal, an increasing trend could indicate a “pile up” of orchestrations in memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-934">當 BizTalk 無法凍結訊息/協調流程執行個體時，可能會發生一段時間遞增趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-934">An increasing trend over time may occur when BizTalk is unable to dehydrate messages/orchestration instances.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-935">嘗試將此計數器與"XLANG/s Orchestrations(?) 相互關聯\Dehydratable 協調流程 」 其中問號 （？） 是相同計數器執行個體，以做為此計數器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-935">Try to correlate this counter with “XLANG/s Orchestrations(?)\Dehydratable orchestrations” where the question mark (?) is the same counter instance as this counter.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-936">如果大量的協調流程是常駐在記憶體中的，如果協調流程數目最少可凍結，則您的協調流程可能會在記憶體中的閒置，而且可能會造成記憶體流失的狀況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-936">If a high number of orchestrations are resident in memory and if a low number of orchestrations are dehydratable, then your orchestrations are likely idle in memory and may cause a memory leak condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-937">如果有的話，請使用這項分析與 「 \XLANG/s 協調流程 （\*） \Idle 協調流程 」 產生關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-937">Use this analysis in correlation with “\XLANG/s Orchestrations(\*)\Idle orchestrations” if present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-938">遞增趨勢 BizTalk 閒置協調流程中的是更好的指標，記憶體流失，因為無法凍結協調流程執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-938">An increasing trend in BizTalk Idle Orchestrations is a better indicator of memory leaks due to the inability to dehydrate orchestration instances.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-939">這項分析會檢查遞增趨勢常駐記憶體，且如果超過 50%的記憶體中駐留的協調流程未凍結的協調流程中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-939">This analysis checks for an increasing trend in orchestrations resident in memory and if more than 50% of the orchestrations resident in memory are not dehydratable.</span></span>

    [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155284](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155284)  
  
## <a name="biztalk-private-bytes-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-943">BizTalk 私用位元組分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-943">BizTalk Private Bytes Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-944">這是主控件執行個體，其相當於"\Process （\*） \Private 位元組 」 效能計數器的配置私用記憶體 mb。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-944">This is the megabytes of allocated private memory for the host instance and comparable to the “\Process(\*)\Private Bytes” performance counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-945">私用位元組是記憶體的目前的大小，以位元組為單位的處理序已配置，不能與其他處理序共用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-945">Private Bytes is the current size, in bytes, of memory that a process has allocated that cannot be shared with other processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-946">這項分析會判斷是否任何主控件執行個體正在耗用龐大的系統記憶體和主控件執行個體是否持續一段時間的記憶體耗用量增加。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-946">This analysis determines whether any of the host instances are consuming a large size of the system's memory and whether the host instance is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-947">耗用記憶體的主控件執行個體是正常的只要它傳回至系統的記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-947">A host instance consuming large portions of memory is fine as long as the it returns the memory to the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-948">尋找增加圖表中的趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-948">Look for increasing trends in the chart.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-949">遞增趨勢上很長一段時間可能表示記憶體流失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-949">An increasing trend over a long period of time could indicate a memory leak.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-950">這項分析會檢查每小時 10 MB-遞增的趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-950">This analysis checks for a 10 MB-per-hour increasing trend.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-951">您可以使用這項分析中可用的記憶體分析與記憶體流失分析相互關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-951">Use this analysis in correlation with the Available Memory analysis and the Memory Leak analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-952">此外，請記住，新啟動主控件執行個體一開始會顯示為記憶體流失時，它只是一般啟動行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-952">Also, keep in mind that newly started host instances will initially appear as a memory leak when it is simply normal start up behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-953">記憶體遺漏時，處理程序會繼續耗用記憶體和沒有釋出一段很長一段時間的記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-953">A memory leak is when a process continues to consume memory and not releasing memory over a long period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-954">如果您懷疑記憶體流失的情況，請閱讀以下參照"記憶體成長中 BizTalk 傳訊 」 文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-954">If you suspect a memory leak condition, then read the “Memory Growth in BizTalk Messaging” article referenced below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-955">否則，安裝並使用偵錯診斷工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-955">Otherwise, install and use the Debug Diag tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-956">如需有關偵錯診斷工具的詳細資訊，請參閱 < 參考一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-956">For more information on the Debug Diag Tool, see the references section.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-virtual-bytes-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-960">BizTalk 虛擬位元組分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-960">BizTalk Virtual Bytes Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-961">這是保留給主控件執行個體的虛擬記憶體 （mb）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-961">This is the megabytes reserved for virtual memory for the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-962">這項分析會決定是否任何主控件執行個體正在耗用大量系統的記憶體，以及是否在經過一段時間的記憶體耗用量增加主控件執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-962">This analysis determines whether any of the host instances are consuming a large amount of the system's memory and whether the host instance is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-963">耗用記憶體的主控件執行個體是正常的只要它會傳回至系統記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-963">A host instance consuming large portions of memory is fine as long as it returns the memory to the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-964">尋找增加圖表中的趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-964">Look for increasing trends in the chart.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-965">遞增趨勢上很長一段時間可能表示記憶體流失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-965">An increasing trend over a long period of time could indicate a memory leak.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-966">這項分析會檢查每小時 10 MB-遞增的趨勢，以虛擬位元組為單位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-966">This analysis checks for a 10 MB-per-hour increasing trend in virtual bytes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-967">您可以使用這項分析中可用的記憶體分析與記憶體流失分析相互關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-967">Use this analysis in correlation with the Available Memory analysis and the Memory Leak analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-968">此外，請記住，新啟動主控件執行個體一開始會顯示為記憶體流失時，它只是一般啟動行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-968">Also, keep in mind that newly started host instances will initially appear as a memory leak when it is simply normal start up behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-969">記憶體遺漏時，處理程序會繼續耗用記憶體和沒有釋出一段很長一段時間的記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-969">A memory leak is when a process continues to consume memory and not releasing memory over a long period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-970">如果您懷疑記憶體流失的狀況，然後讀取 「 記憶體成長中 BizTalk 傳訊 」 下列文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-970">If you suspect a memory leak condition, then read the “Memory Growth in BizTalk Messaging” article below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-971">否則，安裝並使用偵錯診斷工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-971">Otherwise, install and use the Debug Diag tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-972">如需有關偵錯診斷工具的詳細資訊，請參閱 < 參考一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-972">For more information on the Debug Diag Tool, see the references section.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-message-agent-database-session-throttling-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-976">BizTalk 訊息代理程式的資料庫工作階段節流分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-976">BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-977">這是到 MessageBox，相較於其各自的 BizTalk 節流設定的開放式資料庫連接的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-977">This is the number of open database connections to the MessageBox compared to its respective BizTalk throttling setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-978">「 資料庫每一 CPU 的連線 」 為並行資料庫工作階段數目上限 （每一 CPU) 節流開始前允許。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-978">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-979">一般個別主控件工作階段集區中的閒置資料庫工作階段不會加到此計數，而是對主控件執行個體實際正在使用的工作階段數目嚴格執行這項檢查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-979">The idle database sessions in the common per-host session pool do not add to this count, and this check is made strictly on the number of sessions actually being used by the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-980">此選項預設為停用；通常只有在資料庫伺服器是 BizTalk Server 系統中的瓶頸時，才應啟用此設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-980">This option is disabled by default; typically this setting should only be enabled if the database server is a bottleneck in the BizTalk Server system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-981">您可以使用 biztalk： 訊息代理程式的效能物件類別下的資料庫工作階段效能計數器監視使用中的資料庫連線數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-981">You can monitor the number of active database connections by using the database session performance counter under the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-982">此參數只會影響輸出訊息節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-982">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-983">輸入值為 0 時可停用以資料庫工作階段數目為基礎的節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-983">Enter a value of 0 to disable throttling that is based on the number of database sessions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-984">預設值是 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-984">The default value is 0.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-985">MaxWorkerThreads 登錄機碼具有數字的執行緒可用來 BizTalk 的影響力，並有助於在其中大部分的 BizTalk 的執行緒都是使用資料庫連接忙碌的情況下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-985">The MaxWorkerThreads registry key has influence on the number threads available to BizTalk and may help in the case where most of BizTalk’s threads are busy with database connections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-986">這項分析會檢查到 MessageBox 的開放式資料庫連接的數目是否大於 80%的資料庫工作階段，節流設定，表示可能節流狀況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-986">This analysis checks whether the number of open database connections to the MessageBox are greater than 80 percent of the Database Session Throttling setting, indicating a throttling condition is likely.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-message-agent-database-session-throttling-threshold-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-991">BizTalk 訊息代理程式的資料庫工作階段節流閾值分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-991">BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling Threshold Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-992">這是到 MessageBox 的開放式資料庫連接數目的目前閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-992">This is the current threshold for the number of open database connections to the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-993">「 資料庫每一 CPU 的連線 」 為並行資料庫工作階段數目上限 （每一 CPU) 節流開始前允許。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-993">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-994">一般個別主控件工作階段集區中的閒置資料庫工作階段不會加到此計數，而是對主控件執行個體實際正在使用的工作階段數目嚴格執行這項檢查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-994">The idle database sessions in the common per-host session pool do not add to this count, and this check is made strictly on the number of sessions actually being used by the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-995">此選項預設為停用；通常只有在資料庫伺服器是 BizTalk Server 系統中的瓶頸時，才應啟用此設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-995">This option is disabled by default; typically this setting should only be enabled if the database server is a bottleneck in the BizTalk Server system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-996">您可以使用 biztalk： 訊息代理程式的效能物件類別下的資料庫工作階段效能計數器監視使用中的資料庫連線數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-996">You can monitor the number of active database connections by using the database session performance counter under the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-997">此參數只會影響輸出訊息節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-997">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-998">輸入值為 0 時可停用以資料庫工作階段數目為基礎的節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-998">Enter a value of 0 to disable throttling that is based on the number of database sessions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-999">預設值是 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-999">The default value is 0.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1000">MaxWorkerThreads 登錄機碼具有數字的執行緒可用來 BizTalk 的影響力，並有助於在其中大部分的 BizTalk 的執行緒都是使用資料庫連接忙碌的情況下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1000">The MaxWorkerThreads registry key has influence on the number threads available to BizTalk and may help in the case where most of BizTalk’s threads are busy with database connections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1001">這項分析會檢查此值來查看是否有已修改的預設設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1001">This analysis checks this value to see whether it has been modified from its default setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1002">根據預設，此設定會是 0，表示節流的資料庫工作階段上已停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1002">By default, this setting is 0, which means throttling on database sessions is disabled.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-message-agent-in-process-message-count-throttling-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1007">BizTalk 訊息代理程式內含式訊息計數節流分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1007">BizTalk Message Agent In-process Message Count Throttling Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1008">這是並行服務類別正在處理的訊息數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1008">This is the number of concurrent messages that the service class is processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1009">「 內含式訊息每一 CPU 」 中的設定主控件節流設定是傳遞至 「 結束點管理員 」 (EPM) 或 XLANG 尚未處理的訊息的數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1009">The “In-process messages per CPU” setting in the Host Throttling Settings is the maximum number of messages delivered to the End Point Manager (EPM) or XLANG that have not been processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1010">這不包括從資料庫擷取但仍在等候記憶體中的佇列中傳遞的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1010">This does not include the messages retrieved from the database but still waiting for delivery in the in-memory queue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1011">您可以使用 biztalk： 訊息代理程式的效能物件類別下的 內含式訊息計數 效能計數器來監視內含式訊息的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1011">You can monitor the number of in-process messages by using the In-process message count performance counter under the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1012">此參數提供提示給節流機制，做為節流狀況的考量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1012">This parameter provides a hint to the throttling mechanism for consideration of throttling conditions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1013">實際閾值會受自我調整影響而不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1013">The actual threshold is subject to self-tuning.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1014">您可以監視內含式訊息計數效能計數器，以確認實際閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1014">You can verify the actual threshold by monitoring the In-process message count performance counter.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1015">對於大型訊息實例 （其中平均訊息大小很高，或訊息的處理可能需要大量的訊息），這個參數可以設定為較小的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1015">For large message scenarios (where either the average message size is high, or the processing of messages may require a large amount of messages), this parameter can be set to a smaller value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1016">大型訊息實例被表示如果記憶體為根據的節流太過頻繁發生且臨界值時，取得自動調整為相當低的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1016">A large message scenario is indicated if memory-based throttling occurs too often and if the memory threshold gets auto-adjusted to a substantially low value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1017">此類行為發生時表示輸出傳輸應減少同時處理的訊息數，以避免過度使用記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1017">Such behavior would indicate that the outbound transport should process fewer messages concurrently to avoid excessive memory usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1018">此外，對於一次處理少量訊息可讓配接器較有效率的實例 (例如，傳送至限制並行連線的伺服器時)，此參數可調整為低於預設的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1018">Also, for scenarios where the adapter is more efficient when processing a few messages at a time (for example, when sending to a server that limits concurrent connections), this parameter may be tuned to a lower value than the default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1019">這項分析會檢查高內含式訊息計數計數器來判斷其是否超過其節流設定相同的名稱下的 80%，表示節流狀況有可能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1019">This analysis checks the High In-Process Message Count counter to determine whether it is greater than 80 percent of its throttling setting under the same name, which indicates a throttling condition is likely.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="references"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1020">參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1020">References</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1031">對於大型訊息實例 （其中平均訊息大小很高，或訊息的處理可能需要大量的訊息），這個參數可以設定為較小的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1031">For large message scenarios (where either the average message size is high, or the processing of messages may require a large amount of messages), this parameter can be set to a smaller value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1032">大型訊息實例被表示如果記憶體為根據的節流太過頻繁發生且臨界值時，取得自動調整為相當低的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1032">A large message scenario is indicated if memory-based throttling occurs too often and if the memory threshold gets auto-adjusted to a substantially low value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1033">此類行為發生時表示輸出傳輸應減少同時處理的訊息數，以避免過度使用記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1033">Such behavior would indicate that the outbound transport should process fewer messages concurrently to avoid excessive memory usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1034">此外，對於一次處理少量訊息可讓配接器較有效率的實例 (例如，傳送至限制並行連線的伺服器時)，此參數可調整為低於預設的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1034">Also, for scenarios where the adapter is more efficient when processing a few messages at a time (for example, when sending to a server that limits concurrent connections), this parameter may be tuned to a lower value than the default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1035">這項分析會檢查節流處理臨界值的非預設值高內含式訊息計數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1035">This analysis checks the High In-Process Message Count throttling threshold for a non-default value.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1038">如何修改預設主控件節流設定 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155296](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155296)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1038">How to Modify the Default Host Throttling Settings at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155296](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155296)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="biztalk-message-agent-process-memory-usage-mb-throttling-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1039">BizTalk 訊息代理程式處理序記憶體使用量 (MB) 節流分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1039">BizTalk Message Agent Process Memory Usage (MB) Throttling Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1040">這是目前的處理序 (MB) 的記憶體使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1040">This is the memory usage of current process (MB).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1041">BizTalk 處理序記憶體節流設定可能要發行批次具有並不容易學習的記憶體需求，或是太多的執行緒正在處理訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1041">BizTalk process memory throttling can occur if the batch to be published has steep memory requirements, or if too many threads are processing messages.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1042">若系統出現過度節流，請考慮增加主控件相關聯處理序記憶體使用量閾值的值，並確認主控件執行個體不會產生 「 記憶體不足 」 錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1042">If the system appears to be over-throttling, consider increasing the value associated with the process memory usage threshold for the host and verify that the host instance does not generate an "out of memory" error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1043">如果藉由增加程序記憶體使用量閾值，會引發 「 記憶體不足 」 錯誤，請考慮縮減內部訊息佇列大小的值，內含式訊息，每個 CPU 臨界值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1043">If an "out of memory" error is raised by increasing the process memory usage threshold, then consider reducing the values for the internal message queue size and in-process messages per CPU thresholds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1044">此策略特別會與大型訊息處理實例有關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1044">This strategy is particularly relevant in large message processing scenarios.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1045">如果您的 BizTalk server 定期執行虛擬記憶體不足，請考慮 BizTalk Server 64 位元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1045">If your BizTalk server regularly runs out of virtual memory, then consider BizTalk Server 64-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1046">在 64 位元伺服器上的每個處理序可以處理最多 4 TB 的虛擬記憶體與 2 GB 的 32 位元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1046">Each Process on 64-bit servers can address up to 4 TB’s of virtual memory versus the 2 GB’s in 32-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1047">一般情況下，強烈建議 BizTalk 64 位元和 64 位元 SQL Server。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1047">In general, 64-bit BizTalk and 64-bit SQL Server is highly recommended.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1048">請參閱 < BizTalk Server 64 位元支援 > 參考，如需詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1048">See the “BizTalk Server 64-bit Support” reference for more information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1049">這項分析會檢查是否大於 80%的其各自的節流臨界值具有相同名稱的程序記憶體使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1049">This analysis checks whether the process memory usage is greater than 80 percent of its respective throttling threshold of the same name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1050">根據預設，節流設定的 BizTalk 程序記憶體使用量會是 25%之處理序可用的虛擬記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1050">By default, the BizTalk Process Memory Usage throttling setting is 25 percent of the virtual memory available to the process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1051">/3GB 參數這項設定沒有作用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1051">The /3GB switch has no effect on this setting.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalkmessage-agent-process-memory-usage-mb-throttling-threshold-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1057">Biztalk： 訊息代理程式處理序記憶體使用量 (MB) 節流閾值分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1057">BizTalk:Message Agent Process Memory Usage (MB) Throttling Threshold Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1058">這是目前的處理序 (MB) 的記憶體使用量的目前閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1058">This is the current threshold for the memory usage of current process (MB).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1059">實際至這個處理序記憶體耗用量模式，其可用的記憶體數量而定，可能會以動態方式調整臨界值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1059">The threshold may be dynamically adjusted depending on the actual amount of memory available to this process and its memory consumption pattern.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1060">BizTalk 處理序記憶體節流設定可能要發行批次具有並不容易學習的記憶體需求，或是太多的執行緒正在處理訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1060">BizTalk process memory throttling can occur if the batch to be published has steep memory requirements, or if too many threads are processing messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1061">若系統出現過度節流，請考慮增加主控件相關聯處理序記憶體使用量閾值的值，並確認主控件執行個體不會產生 「 記憶體不足 」 錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1061">If the system appears to be over-throttling, consider increasing the value associated with the process memory usage threshold for the host and verify that the host instance does not generate an "out of memory" error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1062">如果藉由增加程序記憶體使用量閾值，會引發 「 記憶體不足 」 錯誤，請考慮縮減內部訊息佇列大小的值，內含式訊息，每個 CPU 臨界值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1062">If an "out of memory" error is raised by increasing the process memory usage threshold, then consider reducing the values for the internal message queue size and in-process messages per CPU thresholds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1063">此策略特別會與大型訊息處理實例有關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1063">This strategy is particularly relevant in large message processing scenarios.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1064">如果您的 BizTalk server 定期執行虛擬記憶體不足，請考慮 BizTalk Server 64 位元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1064">If your BizTalk server regularly runs out of virtual memory, then consider BizTalk Server 64-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1065">在 64 位元伺服器上的每個處理序可以處理最多 4 TB 的虛擬記憶體與 2 GB 的 32 位元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1065">Each Process on 64-bit servers can address up to 4 TB’s of virtual memory versus the 2 GB’s in 32-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1066">一般情況下，強烈建議 BizTalk 64 位元和 64 位元 SQL Server。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1066">In general, 64-bit BizTalk and 64-bit SQL Server is highly recommended.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1067">請參閱 < BizTalk Server 64 位元支援 > 參考，如需詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1067">See the “BizTalk Server 64-bit Support” reference for more information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9fc74-1068">這項分析會檢查是否程序記憶體節流設定為非預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9fc74-1068">This analysis checks whether the Process memory throttling is set to a non-default value.</span></span>
